Major Dark Secrets of American Banking Speculation

Is Mussolini Also Taking Public Bonds? 74

Startling Exposures in the Morgan Case

(National News, Washington, 2nd) At a time when the US Senate is thoroughly investigating the methods by which bankers profit in the securities market, hoping to design measures to curb speculation, it is unexpected that the American public is flocking to the stock exchanges in major ports, hoping to strike it rich. Although no one dares to say that what the Senate committee has discovered has had the unintended effect of encouraging people to try again, the crowd of participants in transactions in the exchanges today is unprecedented since 1929. Leading speculators have consistently bought in, causing the price on the New York Stock Exchange to increase by one pound sterling to as much as nine pounds sterling. The offices of brokers are filled with male and female clients, all eager to choose stable securities and buy them. Even the commodities market is active as a result. As the Senate continues to thoroughly investigate the Morgan Banking Corporation today, it has been discovered that Morgan Bank and six other banks jointly acquired 1,146,609 shares when the securities market collapsed in 1929 with no way to raise it, in an attempt to save the market from collapse. Subsequently, when market prices rose slightly in 1930, they sold them and made a profit of $1,067,355. Suddenly, Senator McCreitz asked whether the account books of those enjoying special rights from the company included the names of King Vittorio Emanuele, Mussolini, and the British royal family. Investigator Picola replied that he had not seen them. Morgan Corporation shareholder Whitley replied that he did not know whether European royalty had stock accounts made on their behalf, but that there was no way to tell if there were no such arrangements. Subsequently, it was also discovered that the list of those favored by Morgan included famous American figures, from retiring presidents to political operatives, without exception. However, no foreign dignitaries have been discovered to date. Whenever there are securities that can be speculated on, the company notifies these individuals, who can often purchase them from Morgan Bank at prices far below market value.

(Reuters, Washington, 2nd) The rumor that Morgan Company sold securities at reduced prices to King Vittorio Emanuele and French politicians drew general attention today during the Senate's review of Morgan's business activities. This claim was made by Senator Reynolds, but Morgan Company shareholder Whitney strongly denied it and promised to present a list showing how securities sent to England and France were distributed. Reynolds's question contained political implications, suggesting that international bankers such as Morgan Company were lobbying to cancel war debts in order to protect their investments in Europe. Whitney replied that he believed the distribution of stocks had nothing to do with war debts and did not harm American interests.

(Reuters, New York, 2nd) The grand jury today brought another public lawsuit against Harriman, the manager of the former Harriman National Bank and Trust Company, for falsifying bank records. It is reported that Harriman was charged in March of this year for falsifying records totaling $1,661,000 in an attempt to deceive currency accountants. After being charged, he was released on bail. He suddenly disappeared last month but was eventually found by police in the Rosslyn Hotel on Catalina Island. When the police arrived at the hotel, Harriman cried and stabbed himself in the heart with a knife in an attempt to commit suicide. He was then sent to Manila Hospital for treatment. Harriman left a letter in the room asking someone to inform his relatives. The next day, the authorities immediately ordered that if Harriman attempted to escape, he should be arrested.

Major Fire at American Oil Field

Millions of Gallons of Kerosene Poured into the Pacific 75

Ten Major Oil Wells Blaze into the Sky

The Flames Spread, Turning the Area into a Sea of Fire

Reports of Twenty Fatalities

(National News, Long Beach (California), 2nd) A major fire broke out at the famous Signal Hill oil field here this afternoon. Flames from ten major oil wells shot into the sky. The wind fanned the flames, spreading the fire toward the oil storage tanks. As a result, fire-fighting forces, the army, and the police were divided into two groups. One group closed off the oil wells that were already on fire and those that were not yet on fire, and the other group opened the oil tanks, pouring millions of gallons of kerosene into the Pacific Ocean. In addition, because the existing pipelines for transporting kerosene to ships were not discharging quickly enough, holes were drilled in the bottom of the tanks, allowing the kerosene to flow through two city streets into the ocean. At one point, the oil was two feet deep in the streets. Although this loss is significant, it prevented the entire mine from being completely destroyed. The rescue efforts were largely extinguished by the evening, with only a few wells still smoldering. The fire was caused by an explosion at a distillery. The force of the explosion shook the area within a twenty-five-mile radius. Three hundred sailors not far from the oil field were knocked to the ground. There are reports of twenty fatalities, and seven bodies have already been recovered. The flames spread from the oil factory to the oil wells and the accumulated waste oil on the ground, turning the area into a sea of fire. Fortunately, large contingents of military police arrived to rescue within a few minutes.

(Reuters, Long Beach, California, 3rd) An explosion at the refinery of the Richfield Oil Company in the United States today killed eleven people and injured eighteen. The sound of the explosion was heard thirty miles around, and the damage is estimated at $1 million.

Another American Initiative 76

Participating in the International Labor Conference

(Reuters, Geneva, 2nd) The US government today appointed William Green of the American Federation of Labor and Miss Anderson, director of the Women's Bureau of the Department of Labor, to participate in the International Labor Conference to be held on June 8. This is an American initiative and another important sign that the United States is abandoning its traditional policy of non-interference in European affairs.

Bankers' Berlin Conference Concludes

Decision on Germany's Debt Relief Measures 77

France Believes it Does Not Affect the Young Plan

(Reuters, Berlin, 2nd) A deferred payment plan for Germany's long-term and short-term foreign debt is expected to be announced soon, approximately after Pentecost. This statement was made today by Schacht, the president of the German National Bank, to foreign journalists here. The meeting of foreign bankers in Berlin concluded today. Schacht explained the significance of this meeting, saying that the German National Bank has firmly decided not to allow its foreign currency reserves to shrink further, and that ordinary import and export credit must be maintained. Germany is willing to repay its debts but must have the opportunity to earn money to pay them. The stability of the German currency must be maintained under any circumstances. The importance of Schacht's remarks about debt relief can be seen in the amount of debt that Germany must repay this year. The total amount of German debt is approximately 20,000,000,000 marks, of which 65,000,000 pounds are due this year. The largest debt is owed to the United States, totaling 8,016,000,000 marks, followed by the Netherlands, totaling 3,427,000,000 marks, and then the United Kingdom, totaling 2,231,000,000 marks. The current difficulty is due to the significant decline in German trade. The National Bank's banknote reserve is only 8.3%, while the statutory minimum reserve is 40%. Although Schacht did not explicitly state a deferral of payment, those who heard his words interpreted it that way. The foreign bankers' conference, which considered the matter of Germany's foreign debt repayment, unanimously passed a document today expressing agreement on the need for the German National Bank to gradually increase its cash and foreign currency reserves and acknowledging the need to consider how to protect and expand Germany's foreign exchange reserves due to the decrease in Germany's foreign trade surplus, which is insufficient to repay its debts. The document also announced that a permanent small group representing long-term creditors would be in constant contact with the German National Bank, and that short-term creditors would also have a fixed committee in contact with the bank. The document concluded that international debt issues could only be resolved by the flow of goods and the reorganization of debt repayment methods, and it was believed that one of the greatest objectives of the World Economic Conference would be to facilitate the rapid and permanent resolution of Germany's transit problems.

(Reuters, Berlin, 2nd) It is expected that a debt relief measure will be announced next week, but it is not a general relief. Schacht will announce a deferral of principal repayment but will endeavor to repay part of the interest in foreign currency, with the remaining interest to be repaid in marks that must be used in Germany. As for the repayment of the Dawes and Young loans, they are not affected at present. American representatives attending the bankers' conference have stated that if Schacht announces a general moratorium, American bondholders are prepared to seize any assets in the United States of German businesses that do not pay their bonds.

(Reuters, Paris, 2nd) The official sector here has expressed little reaction to the remarks of Schacht, president of the German National Bank, believing that these remarks refer only to the German government's private debts and do not involve the bonds of the Young Plan.

(Reuters, Berlin, 3rd) German newspapers commenting on the debt relief measures to be announced stated that the plan foreshadowed by Schacht, president of the National Bank, is absolutely necessary and must be implemented for the sake of protecting both creditors and debtors until an agreement is reached with creditors on a solution that Germany can tolerate. The Börsen-Zeitung stated that the final decision on Germany's ability to pay its debts belongs to the World Economic Conference. If the conference properly manages international trade relations, its decision will be positive. However, if the politicians of various countries do not replace the current policies with constructive policies, their decision will be negative.

German Ex-Crown Prince's Grandson Marries 78

(Reuters, Pion, 3rd) William, the grandson of the German ex-Crown Prince and the eldest son of the German ex-Prince, married Ms. Cäcilie von Savoie-Aosta here this morning at the town hall. A large crowd watched outside the hall, and the ceremony was simple. The officiant was a registrar official, and the witnesses were the bride's brother and Count von Blumenthal. After the ceremony, they went to the bride's mother's house in the same car for a religious wedding ceremony. The bride is a descendant of Italian nobles who later moved to Germany. Members of the ex-royal family do not approve of the ex-Crown Prince's grandson marrying a commoner, so if Germany is restored in the future, the ex-Crown Prince's grandson will lose his right to inherit the throne.

Japanese Political Turmoil 79

(Denpō, Tokyo, 3rd) The conflict between the radical and self-respecting factions within the Seiyūkai, led by President Suzuki Kisaburō, regarding the reorganization of the party, led to a request for mediation from Mochizuki Keisuke. Mochizuki stated that hasty mediation at this time would be inappropriate, so the president postponed a decision, intending to adopt a wait-and-see attitude to understand the party's direction. However, the radical faction, which had previously acknowledged the weakness of the current cabinet at a cadre meeting and decided that the Seiyūkai should adopt a policy of independent progress, now suddenly fears party turmoil and burying itself in doubt, which would be a disgrace to the world, so they are extremely dissatisfied and will begin a fierce resistance movement. In particular, Shimada Toshiwo and Yamaguchi Giichi are enthusiastic about the argument for a national cabinet based on party mergers or party alliances. Yamamoto Jōtarō and other former Seiyūkai members, as well as Kuhara Fusanosuke, have also expressed their support. Even Tokonami Takejirō and Mochizuki, if President Suzuki is determined to do so, will express their support. The argument for a coalition cabinet has gradually gained strength within the party, so the timing of President Suzuki's decision, regardless of its content, is expected to be in early or late June, but may be delayed by one or two months. For the time being, the status quo will be maintained.

(Denpō, Tokyo, 3rd) Seiyūkai elders Okazaki, Mochizuki, and Sunada met at the Kōjunsya this afternoon at 1:30 PM to discuss the issue of severing ties with the government. As a result, they reached a consensus that the party must be united at this time regardless. However, if they disregard the decisions made at the cadre meeting, it will affect the party's credibility, and the arguments of the self-respecting faction are also quite reasonable, so they cannot be ignored. As a result, both factions should show mutual respect and make the best efforts for the future of the party with a compromising attitude.

(Denpō, Tokyo, 3rd) Seiyūkai's radical faction members Sunada Shigemasa and Okada Tadahiko visited President Suzuki this morning at 10:30 AM to state their strong opinions, saying that the self-respecting faction is currently plotting, and they hope to follow the main purpose of the cadre meeting's decision, without harming the party's image, and decisively sever ties with the current cabinet. The severance faction has always wanted to implement its original intentions, while the middle-ranking group gathered at the Kawachiya in Tsukiji tonight, and the radical faction also gathered at the Kōrakukan in Akasaka. The self-respecting faction also gathered at the Miyuki-en in Shiba to discuss.

(Denpō, Tokyo, 3rd) As of last night, the Seiyūkai's self-respecting faction seemed to have the upper hand. The radical faction, stimulated, suddenly turned the tables and is also dissatisfied with Mochizuki, and will take more active actions, deciding on major expansion at Kawachiya and Kōrakukan tonight. Therefore, the power of the severance faction and the self-respecting faction are equal, and the situation is chaotic. President Suzuki will not make an easy decision before clarifying the trend of the general situation. However, since the cadre meeting has already made a decision, he cannot completely ignore it, because it concerns the party's image and the president's prestige. However, the idea of a coalition cabinet will be considered again in the event of a political change, and today's issue is a separate matter.

(Denpō, Tokyo, 3rd) Cabinet Secretary Horiouchi visited Home Minister Yamamoto at 9:00 AM this morning to discuss the policy to be submitted at the next Diet session. In addition to the existing committee members, temporary committee members who are experts should be added to study proportional representation, and the deliberation committee should be opened as soon as possible.

It is reported that Mattern, together with Griffin, set out from New York last July to fly around the world and establish a new record. He arrived in Berlin from the United States several hours earlier than the previous record. He had hoped that a new record could be created, but the plane crashed in Russian territory, and the fuselage was severely damaged and could not continue the flight.

Recent Foreign Trade of the Soviet Union 85

Exports Exceed Imports by Over 23 Million Rubles

(TASS, Moscow) The total value of the Soviet Union's foreign trade in the first quarter of this year was 200,500,000 rubles, of which exports were valued at 112,103,000 rubles and imports were valued at 88,401,000 rubles, resulting in a trade surplus of 23,702,000 rubles. Raw materials and semi-finished products accounted for 61.6% of the value of exports, food accounted for 24.5%, and gold products accounted for 13.9%. Gold products accounted for 59.3% of the value of imports, raw materials and semi-finished products accounted for 33.3%, and food accounted for 3.4%. Soviet Perspective on the World Economic Crisis 86

(TASS, Moscow) An article published in Pravda here laments the terrible state of the capitalist world economic crisis over the past three years, as well as the current destruction of machinery aimed at hindering production and technological progress. Regarding the United States, the newspaper states that even in this most advanced and magnificent capitalist country, various types of production are undergoing unparalleled declines. In 1932, cast iron production was only 80% of that in 1929, equivalent to the level of 1896. During the same period, steel production decreased by 76%. The utilization of open-hearth furnaces was only 14% of their total capacity. The automotive industry, which requires the most metal, produced only 75% of what it did in 1929, so the demand for metal also decreased sharply. Railway transport volume decreased by half, electricity production decreased by 25%, and only one-fifth of the country's electrical industry is operating. The decline in other sectors of the machinery manufacturing industry is even more severe, with many parts only operating at 5% to 10%. Pravda continues, although the development of various countries and sectors of industry in the world is extremely unbalanced, the situation in other capitalist countries is no better than in the United States. The German Economic Research Institute published the following table, indicating the workload of major industries worldwide in 1932:

Coal Mining Industry: 48.7% Machinery Manufacturing Industry: 27.1% Construction Industry: 22.7% Heavy Industry: 31.3% Light Industry: 42.1% Since capitalist countries are unable to utilize one-third of their original production capacity and are unable to sell their mountains of surplus goods, they have no choice but to intensify the destruction of their industrial organizations and destroy their products. Ford recently set up a machine specifically for destroying automobiles in one or two factories. This technical achievement is a clear illustration of the destruction of productive forces in the darkness of capitalism. In the current capitalist arena, all technical considerations and construction work are concentrated on how to destroy active machines and how to limit the development of productive forces. The unity of this contradiction in technical development is most obvious. Capitalism plunges millions of people into a state of unemployment and starvation, and the unemployed and starving masses are not limited to the proletariat. The vast majority of farmers, most of the agency employees, intellectuals, scientists, and engineers are also in this situation.

Agreement Signed, Hearts in Tianjin and Beijing Stabilized 87

Strict Precautions in Beijing, Public Security Uncompromised

Traffic Gradually Resumes Former Appearance

Refugees from War Zones Return in Succession

Special Dispatch from Beijing: The Sino-Japanese armistice issue, after two meetings between representatives Xiong Bin and Okamura, etc., in Tanggu, was signed with extreme speed. The content of the agreement is divided into five articles. Our army will withdraw from the area west and south of the line connecting Yanqing, Changping, Gaoliying, Shunyi, Tongzhou, Xianghe, Baodi, Lintingkou, Ninghe, and Lutai and will not advance further, nor engage in any provocative or disruptive actions. After the above agreement is implemented, the Japanese army will not pursue beyond the line and will automatically return to the Great Wall line. Japanese aircraft will also be allowed to inspect at any time, and China should provide protection. Our representative, after signing yesterday (the 31st) afternoon, immediately returned to Beijing. Although there are still unfinished matters between the Chinese and Japanese armies that need final consultation in Tianjin, the peace movement that has been brewing for many days has finally been successful.

Since the authorities began ceasefire negotiations, the hearts of the Beijing people have been slightly stabilized. After the news of the signing of the agreement was revealed in the newspapers this morning, the momentary feelings of shock and fear completely disappeared. In places such as East and West Chang'an Streets, the traffic was bustling, and a thriving atmosphere suddenly appeared. Modern men and women are active again. Although general entertainment venues have not yet returned to their former appearance, famous actors such as Xun Huisheng, Yang Xiaolou, and Ma Lianliang have all posted playbills and will choose a date to perform. It is expected that peace will be seen again within a few days, and there will be no more loneliness. Japanese military aircraft appeared in the skies over Beijing yesterday and today (the 1st). The time of their arrival has been around 11:00 AM and has never changed. They may still fly in for inspection afterward. Since the purpose is benevolent, the Chinese side should provide protection at all times, so the act of bombing should not occur. The public regards it as a commonplace event, completely different from the nature of the initial sighting of Japanese aircraft, so it can be treated with composure.

Because various counties in Hebei were once battlefields between the Chinese and Japanese armies, civilian dwellings and fields were either occupied by soldiers or destroyed by artillery fire. The people had nowhere to return and fled to Beijing one after another. When the war situation at the front was urgent, the number of refugees arriving in Beijing exceeded tens of thousands. Various parties organized reception centers to take in the old and weak. It is estimated that charitable organizations have established refugee reception centers attached to the Poor People's Warm Factory and reception centers of local associations and the Red Swastika Society, etc. In particular, the Red Swastika Society's organization is the largest in scale. In addition to the New World, there are Guanghua Temple, Longquan Orphanage, Qinglong Bridge, and other places that accommodate refugees. At the peak, it reached more than two thousand people, not including other places. Now that the situation is gradually stabilizing, many refugees have returned home in succession. There are very few refugees left in the reception centers. However, the autumn harvest is hopeless this year, and the future panic in the war zone is difficult to imagine. Various charitable organizations are now planning relief measures in advance, and government offices are also coordinating post-disaster measures. The losses of the people will be difficult to compensate in a short period of time.

Large armies gathered in the suburbs of Beijing, and the locations where they were stationed mostly borrowed civilian houses. Recently, the above situation has also occurred in various places in the city. Although the authorities have ordered relocation, most have not yet moved out. Some troops have also borrowed temples for lodging. There is a shortage of public housing for distribution. The overall discipline is still strict, and there is no disturbance to the people, so the military and civilians can get along fairly well. However, the security in the areas where the troops are stationed is extremely tight. Every night after 8:00 PM, additional sentries are assigned near the garrison, carrying guns and ammunition, to check pedestrians. After 10:00 PM, traffic is prohibited. Therefore, although the curfew time is officially set at 11:00 PM at night, there are few people in the secluded alleys after dusk. In order to protect safety, sandbags that were piled up in front of important places have not been removed. The military and police are stepping up patrol duties every night and are not relaxing at all. Although the Sino-Japanese war has stopped, unscrupulous traitors still have the possibility of acting erratically and must be carefully guarded against. It is heard that Li Jichun and Shi Yousan's gangs are still active. After Shi's failed riot in Tianjin, he has now fled to Qinhuangdao and dares to openly issue conscription notices. The authorities are now trying to crack down on them, and it is expected that it will not affect the current situation. (June 1)

Yan's Attitude in Shanxi Amidst the Changing Situation 88

Representatives from All Sides Gather in Taiyuan

Defensive Arrangements Made for the Shanxi-Suiyuan Border

Correspondence from Taiyuan: The long-silent Taiyuan has recently shown signs of activity due to a telegram from Feng Yuxiang in Zhangjiakou, assuming the position of Commander-in-Chief of the People's Anti-Japanese Allied Army. This kind of brewing had been repeatedly discussed and closely watched by the government in the previous few days. Feng's telegram arrived in Taiyuan on the 27th, and the Suiyuan Pacification Headquarters immediately convened a meeting to discuss countermeasures. However, the outcome of the consultation is rarely known to the outside world. The original text of the telegram was first published by various newspapers on the 29th. At the same time, He Jingwu, Chairman of the Pinghan Railway, also came to Taiyuan from Chiang Kai-shek to visit Yan and discuss the situation. He was in a hurry and only stayed in Taiyuan for one night. When he arrived in Taiyuan last night with Wang Maogong, Director of the Zhengtai Railway Bureau, military and political figures such as Xu Yongchang, Chairman of Shanxi Province, Zhao Daiwen, Chief Counselor of the Suiyuan Pacification Headquarters, Yang Aiyuan, Qingxiang Supervisory Officer, and Rong Honglu, Garrison Commander, all went to the station to greet him. Then, they had a long conversation with the welcomers at the Shanxi Grand Hotel. This morning, He personally visited Yan at the Suiyuan Pacification Headquarters for about two hours, and then took the Zhengtai midday train to leave Taiyuan. Xu, Zhao, Yang, and others all went to the station to see him off. It is unknown what He's mission was and what the outcome of his meeting with Yan was. Yan's attitude is still focused on carrying out his ten-year plan and has little expression on the current situation, with a strong intention to remain silent about politics. However, since Feng's attitude has been clearly expressed, it is worth studying how Shanxi and Chahar, due to their geographical environment, will respond. According to general observations, Shanxi may eventually find it difficult to remain silent. Sun Chu, Commander of the Zhengtai Road Protection Army, was appointed by Yan a few days ago as the Commander of the Shanxi-Chahar-Suiyuan Border Defense. Sun's Ma Brigade departed from Taiyuan to Datong. Sun and Brigade Commander Ma Yanshou also went to Datong together a few days ago to inspect their troops and convene a meeting of officers above the regimental level stationed in that area. It is heard that considerable arrangements have been made for the Shanxi-Suiyuan border defense. Sun's troops remaining in the province have continued to move north in the past day or two. Also, Lu Xiuwen, representative of Song Zheyuan, and Xiang Chengren, representative of Yang Hucheng, also came to Taiyuan today to visit Yan and discuss the situation. The society is paying close attention to the comings and goings of representatives from all sides, because the residents have become startled birds due to years of war, and are therefore uneasy about the recent future situation. (May 30)

National Mining Merchants Conference Concludes 89

Issue 20 Million in Coal Industry Public Bonds

Jointly Establish a Road-Mine Repair Vehicle Committee

Dispatch from Beijing: The National Mining Merchants Representatives Conference convened by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce continued its official meeting in the Ministry's auditorium yesterday (2nd) afternoon. Twenty-nine attendees included representatives of various mining merchants, Liu Chuanshu representing the Jinpu Railway, and Huang Jintao, Director of the Mining Department of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce. The meeting was chaired by Huang Jintao and recorded by Huang Zhong. A total of fifteen important proposals and many temporary motions were passed. It was also decided to issue 20 million in coal industry public bonds and to organize a joint road-mine repair vehicle committee. Eleven articles of the charter were also passed. The meeting concluded at 6:30 PM. The details are recorded as follows:

Various Important Proposals Passed 90

In addition to the proposals to reduce the mineral tax standard to 20/1000 and the freight rate on each road to 5 cents per ton per kilometer, the official meeting held from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM yesterday passed the following proposals from each road: (1) Due to the national industrial and commercial depression and low coal prices, the Ministry of Railways should be requested to reduce freight rates to maintain them. (2) Request the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to investigate the national coal consumption and stipulate the output of each mine to balance supply and demand and maintain the business of each mine. (3) Increase the import tax rate on foreign coal to protect the domestic coal industry. (4) Propose to specially reduce and unify the coal transportation prices on the Zhengtai Road. (5) Request to uniformly allocate vehicles to each mine. (6) Request that the counties be ordered to apportion donations to each mine fairly and equitably in the future to show fairness and reduce all miscellaneous donations. (7) Propose to earnestly relieve each mine to avoid business suspension. (8) Request to approve the minimum monthly transportation volume of Datong coal to avoid winter shortages. (9) Request to reduce the freight charges for Datong coal near Beijing on the Ping Sui Railway to facilitate regulation. (10) The Shandong Provincial Government's collection of coal jin subsidies affects the mining industry, and it is sincerely requested to stop the levy as soon as possible. (11) Propose that the Ministry of Railways classify coke and coal jin as sixth-class goods. (12) The preferential price for coal transportation by the Fuzhong Company of the Ping Han Railway has not yet expired. Please allow it to continue to be effective in order to reduce costs and compete with enemy coal. Please consult the Ministry to instruct the Ministry of Railways to implement it. (13) Each road should uniformly exempt coal trucks and escort tickets from collection to promote national coal and show excellence. If it is unavoidable, please stipulate the lowest price to avoid the road side from gaining the sole profit and the mine side from suffering the sole loss. Please consult the Ministry to instruct the Ministry of Railways to comply. (14) The relationship between Daoqing Road and Zhongyuan Company is too close. Please restore the special price for coal transportation at Daokou Sanliwan and the special price for transfer at the new station from now on to avoid stockpiling costs and alleviate the difficulties of the mine. Please consult the Ministry to order the Ministry of Railways to comply. (15) The prices of coal transportation on the Beijing-Shenyang, Tianjin-Pukou, and Longhai Railways are very high. In order to promote domestic goods and resist foreign coal, they should all be reduced uniformly or specially stipulated. Please consult the Ministry for appropriate discretion.

Issuance of Coal Industry Public Bonds 91

The conference continued its last meeting from 3:30 PM to discuss temporary motions. (1) Measures for cooperation in the production and sales of coal jin (Resolved) Representatives from the production, sales, and transportation parties shall be appointed to plan and handle them in a unified manner. The measures shall be decided after consultation by the representatives appointed by the three parties. (2) The former National Coal Relief Committee recommended that the government issue 20 million in coal industry public bonds. However, the issuance has been delayed. Please ask the Ministry to consult the Ministry of Finance to issue them as soon as possible to provide relief (Resolved) The Ministry of Industry and Commerce shall urge the Ministry of Finance to issue them, and each mine shall be used as a public bond guarantee fund. The method of paying interest shall be negotiated by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and the Ministry of Finance. Then, the organization of the joint road-mine repair vehicle committee was discussed. (Resolved) It shall be organized by one or two representatives from each relevant railway and each coal mine. The eleven articles of the charter were passed on the spot. The content is as follows:

Contents of the Committee Charter 92

Article 1: This committee is organized in accordance with the provisions of Article 3 of the Principles for Repairing Locomotives and Vehicles and is named the Joint Road-Mine Repair Vehicle Committee. Article 2: This committee is composed of a number of representatives from both the road and mine sides, who are responsible for handling matters related to coal transportation, vehicle repair, allocation, and adjustment. Article 3: Each road bureau involved in coal transportation shall send one or two representatives, and the coal mines on each route shall jointly elect two representatives to be jointly responsible for handling matters. Article 4: When any mine encounters transportation difficulties, this committee shall find ways to handle them. Article 5: The methods for repairing vehicles, borrowing money, and repaying money shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of the contract signed with the bank. Article 6: This committee shall have three to five standing committee members, who shall be mutually elected by representatives from both the road and mine sides. Article 7: This committee shall have a number of clerks who shall be responsible for matters related to documents, accounting, statistics, examination, and reporting. Article 8: The address of this committee shall be located at [blank]. Article 9: The expenses of this committee shall be borne separately by the relevant mining merchants. Article 10: The production and sales matters related to coal transportation may be studied by this committee, and suggestions may be made to the competent department at any time for verification. Article 11: The detailed rules for the operation of this committee shall be formulated separately.

Minister of Industry and Commerce Hosts a Banquet for Representatives 93

Chen Gongbo, Minister of Industry and Commerce, in addition to expressing his pleasure that the attending representatives traveled from afar to Beijing to participate in the meeting and jointly accomplish this event, specially hosted a banquet for all the attending representatives at his private residence in Xiangpu Camp at 7:00 PM last night (2nd) to socialize and learned that the mining merchants representatives from each province, except for a part who had already returned north by car last night, the rest were scheduled to return to their posts tomorrow (3rd) morning. (June 3)

Southwest Five Provinces

Planning the Qinzhou-Chongqing Railway 94

Preparatory Committee Established After Several Consultations

Correspondence from Chongqing: The joint planning of the Qinzhou-Chongqing Railway by Sichuan, Guizhou, Yunnan, Guangdong, and Guangxi provinces has been publicized for a long time. Representatives from the five provinces had several consultations in Guangzhou, which were quite promising, and a preparatory committee was established to carry out various tasks. Chen Jitang of Guangdong, in order to promote the realization of the road in the shortest possible time, sent representatives Mai Huanzhang and Hu Weisan from Guangdong to Sichuan to contact the military leaders in Sichuan. After Mai and Hu arrived in Chongqing, they immediately visited Liu Xiang, the Pacification Director of Sichuan, to discuss various matters, which was quite satisfactory. Liu agreed to allocate 1 million yuan of railway shares and expressed his willingness to fully support the realization of the road. Mai and Hu then rushed to Chengdu to ask Liu Wenhui of the 24th Army, Deng Xihou of the 28th Army, and Tian Songyao of the 29th Army to express their sympathy and support for the road construction. However, after several visits, there was no satisfactory reply, because the generals of the province were currently busy solving their own survival problems and had no time to take care of road construction. Mai and Hu then went to Qingcheng for sightseeing and planned to visit Mount Emei, but they returned to Chongqing due to the war. According to reports, the authorities in Guangdong and Guangxi have detailed regulations for the road construction plan. Guangdong and Guangxi are responsible for self-construction. The section from Sanshui to Wuzhou already has a railway. An Xingye Bank has been established with a capital of 8 million yuan, which is borne by Guangdong for 5 million yuan and Guangxi for 3 million yuan. In the future, this will be used as a road construction fund. After the successful opening of the section from Sanshui to Wuzhou, the income will be used to gradually plan other sections. When there is insufficient funding, small loans can be made to overseas Chinese, and negotiations can be made with foreign merchants to order rails and vehicles. If foreign merchants can provide assistance and are willing to lend money for rails and vehicles, the progress will be smoother. As for the route problem, Yunnan insisted on first repairing the section from Kunming to Qinzhou, because Qinzhou is China's own seaport. If the section from Kunming to Sichuan is repaired first, it is equivalent to extending the French Yunnan-Vietnam railway and increasing its power to invade the hinterland. Therefore, if Yunnan is passed without repairing the seaport for Yunnan first, Yunnan will definitely disagree. The current plan is to start from Sanshui on the Guangzhou-Sanshui Road, pass through Wuzhou and Liuzhou in Guangxi, and enter Guizhou, pass through Guiyang and enter Chongqing and Chengdu in Sichuan, and then connect to Kunming in Yunnan west of Guiyang and reach Changsha in southern Hunan. However, each section of this route may be separately funded and started. Those with surplus funds will start first, and then plan to extend them. Generally speaking, the cost of building the Qinzhou-Chongqing Railway is about 200,000 yuan per mile (about three Chinese miles). If there is already a road foundation, the cost will be greatly reduced. (May 29)

Huai River Commission Investigation

Water Conservancy Projects in Various Counties Along the Huai River in Shandong Province 95

Correspondence from Jinan: The Huai River Basin concerns the interests of several provinces. The Huai River Commission has been actively preparing for rectification over the years and is now investigating the relevant water conservancy projects in each county for reference. The provincial government of this province received a consultation from the association yesterday, roughly saying that all water conservancy projects belonging to the Huai River Basin are closely related to the Huai River planning of the association. In recent years, there must be many places where the local government and the people can concentrate their efforts to effectively implement the river channels, ponds, and embankments within the territory. The association wants to clarify the implementation results of the water conservancy projects in various places along the Huai River for reference, and specially formulated a survey form on the overview of the water conservancy projects in each county and consulted the noble provincial government to order the competent authorities to print and distribute the form sent by the association to the counties along the Huai River under its jurisdiction and order them to conduct detailed surveys and send them directly to the association for collation, and also order each county to report any water conservancy projects that are continued to be undertaken in the future. According to this, the provincial government should order the Construction Department to investigate and handle it. After receiving the order, the Construction Department should take the Grand Canal, Si River, Yi River, and Shu River in the southwest of the province as the upper reaches of the Huai River and have a network connection with the Huai River. Then, according to the Yun River, Si River, Yi River, Shu River, and other twenty-nine counties, according to the survey form on the overview of local water conservancy projects sent by the Huai River Association, the inquiry should be completed and reported to the department within ten days of the arrival of the document so that it can be collected and forwarded to the association. Labor-Capital Dispute at Hankou Zhenhuan Factory Resolved 98

Work Resumption Scheduled as Result of Labor-Capital Negotiations

Minsheng Textile Company Announces Another Shutdown

Correspondence from Hankou: After the 3,000 workers of Zhenhuan Yarn Factory appealed and the Provincial Party Department and the Provincial Government accepted the request, they ordered the factory to resume operation. Labor and capital, and representatives of various parties, held negotiations. The Construction Department and the Trade Union also sent representatives to participate. After several consultations, two compromise solutions were decided: (1) It was stipulated that one and a half months would be the shutdown period for the factory to clear accounts and raise additional capital, until July 14th. Work will officially resume on the 15th. (2) During the shutdown period, the factory will pay a subsidy of 40% of the total monthly wages of the workers to maintain the workers' lives. Both parties agreed, signed on the 30th, and reported it to the Party, government, and military agencies for record. The turmoil was peacefully resolved. But just as one wave subsided, another wave rose. Minsheng Yarn Factory suddenly decided to shut down on June 1st due to poor business operations and separately submitted reports to the Finance and Construction Departments on the 30th, stating that they would stop paying rent from June 1st (the factory was originally owned by the province, and the Minsheng Company was leasing it from the provincial government). According to the factory, on April 30th, wages were reduced, and salary deductions caused a conflict with the workers, which led to the military police opening fire and causing a tragedy. Not even a month later, it was announced that it would shut down, which was not what the workers were willing to accept. The labor unrest in Wuhan may be on the rise. (May 30)

Songjiang

Rice Mill Workers Open Coffin for Inspection 99

Chen Zhongchao, a native of Jiangbei, at Fei Tongxing Rice Mill outside the South Gate's Datie Bridge, started a fight with Ji Yaohua and Bian Hongkui over gambling debts. Chen fell ill and died. His brother, Zhongjie, according to his fellow villager Liu Jingshou, was willing to testify and reported to the Prosecutor's Office for investigation. Today (the 3rd) at 8:00 AM, Prosecutor Zhu, together with Secretary Qian and the inspectors, rushed to the Second District Office to summon a group of witnesses, ordered the coffin to be opened for inspection, and verified that there were slight injuries on the neck of the deceased, but they were not fatal. The cause of death was clarified, and the local police were ordered to coffin and bury the body, and the suspects Liu and Ji were taken back into custody for interrogation.

Suzhou

Traitor Hu Lifu Executed by Hanging 100

After Hu Lifu, a traitor, was arrested in Shanghai and sent to the Jiangsu Higher Court for trial, he was sentenced to life imprisonment. Hu immediately declared his disagreement and appealed to the Supreme Court. He was then sentenced by the court to revoke the judgment of the first instance and change the sentence to Hu Lifu's death. The judgment was sent to Hu's family by the Suzhou Higher Court the day before yesterday. Yesterday (the 3rd) morning, the Procuratorate of the Higher Court received an order from the Ministry to execute Hu and executed it at 1:30 PM under the supervision of Prosecutor Zhu Wenzhuo, the supervising execution officer, to the Third Prison on Siqian Street to bring Hu out to verify his identity. When the traitor Hu Lifu was executed by hanging (photographed by Lin Xuehuai), he found 10 yuan in his pocket. Hu knew that his death day had arrived, and he could not help but feel sad and shed tears. Before the execution, the supervising execution officer asked if there were any last words. Hu shook his head and sighed and said, "I sold the land to relieve the refugees. Now I have such a result. It is really dark and there is no day. What else is there to say? I can only go to the underworld to file a complaint." He only asked the court to send a letter to his family in Shanghai to come and collect the body and instructed them to be buried in his hometown. After saying that, he kept shaking his head. The supervising execution officer then ordered Hu to be hoisted onto the gallows and executed by hanging according to the law.

Wuxi

Bandit Gang Robbery and Assault 101

In the first district of this county, Youdu Village, 584th map, the second house west of the bridge, villager Lu Panfu, is currently a foreman at the Qingfeng Yarn Factory, and his son Agou is a worker in the fine yarn section of the Guangqin Yarn Factory. Their family life is barely sustainable. Agou got married in March of this year. Yesterday (the 3rd) at 1:00 AM, suddenly six bandits, each wielding a handgun, arrived at the village. First, they opened the front door of the neighboring first house, the home of You Asan. You heard the noise and went to investigate, but was shot in the abdomen by the bandits. The bullet entered his waist and did not exit. Immediately afterward, they opened the Lu family's front door. Two bandits stood guard outside, while four bandits entered the house. First, they went to Lu Panfu's bedroom on the front floor to rob him, then they went to Lu Agou's room on the back floor to search and plunder. Agou put up some resistance and was also shot, the bullet entering his nose and exiting his neck. He fell to the ground in a pool of blood, unconscious. They robbed him of forty-three yuan in cash, a watch, and some Xiangyun gauze clothing, for a total loss of over one hundred yuan. After obtaining their loot, the bandits fled toward the Lengdu Harbor area. After the incident, You and Lu were injured. Their family members carried them to the city overnight and admitted them to Puren Hospital for treatment. According to the doctors, You Asan's injuries are light and should not be a major concern. Lu Agou's injuries are very serious and may be life-threatening. Yu Shuming, a patrol officer from the first police substation directly under the jurisdiction of the area, upon hearing about the major robbery and assault case, immediately led police officers to investigate the scene. They found five spent handgun cartridges left behind by the bandits. While pursuing the stolen goods and robbers, they apprehended one suspect and took him into custody. Furthermore, at Liu Fuquan's home in Hui Lane, Lengdu Township, 587th map of the second district, several bandits also arrived that evening and robbed them of a pair of gold bracelets and several articles of clothing. Additionally, at the home of Hua Yaoyu, a resident of Changjiang Village near Zhangcun Town in the fifth district, over ten bandits climbed over the wall and entered, stealing over one hundred yuan.

Changzhou

Cocoon Market Conditions in Various Townships 102

The Wuyi four-township cocoon market is most prosperous in the southeast township. Due to the impact of last year's declining cocoon market, the number of silk farmers in the northwest and northeast townships is very small this spring. However, the quality of fresh cocoons produced in various townships this year is good. Although there are fewer farmers, the output is still good. There are over 170 cocoon merchants in the county, with about two-thirds having opened for business. In the eastern township, the Henglin Qishuyan area opened for business on June 1st. There was not much activity until the 2nd. Today (the 3rd) there are more goods arriving. Native cocoons are around thirty yuan, and improved varieties are around forty yuan. The western township opened for business one day later than the eastern township. As of the 2nd, there were still not many goods being collected.

Nantong

Lusi Soldier Mutiny Relief Standards 103

In Nantong's Lusi, after merchants and residents were robbed by mutinous soldiers from the Provincial Security Coastal Patrol Brigade, the county government, following provincial orders, investigated and found that merchants and residents had lost a total of 240,000 yuan. It also formulated relief standards: those who are extremely poor will receive full relief, and those who are less poor will receive 70% relief. The list will be submitted to the province for review and approval.

Jiangyin

Investigation of Smoking Leads to a Death 104

The fourth anti-narcotics division of this county has a branch in Jingjiang. On the 30th of last month, Zhang Luxuan, the acting director, sent personnel to the Yin family west of the Liedi Temple outside the north gate to search for opium, but found nothing. They arrested Wei Qinglang, a servant of the family, and took him to the branch, where he was subjected to private torture and beatings. He died at midnight. Later, the body was suddenly discovered in Yangshi Harbor. One morning, a trash picker named Shi Shunlang spotted it and reported it to the Public Security Bureau. The incident alarmed the public, who flocked to the anti-narcotics division and the Hefeng Opium Company. Over ten employees and officers were arrested and placed under the custody of the Public Security Bureau. On the 1st, County Magistrate Chen appointed Judge Bao and Examiner Cao to go to the west gate to examine the body. The examination revealed that the deceased had a wooden stick injury on his right forehead, two wooden stick injuries on his left ribs, a fist injury on his right ribs, and two stabbing injuries on his arm. It was determined that the injuries were inflicted before death, and the deceased fell into the river and died. After the examination, the deceased's wife, Wang, collected the body. At 1:00 PM, the Public Security Bureau transferred the personnel from the anti-narcotics division and the Hefeng Opium Company to the county, where they were interrogated by Judge Bao. Zhang Luxuan and others only admitted that after Wei Qinglang was arrested, he was handed over to Zhang Jingran for custody and then locked in a detention center. They claimed that they did not interrogate him and were unaware of his disappearance at 3:00 PM on the 31st. They suggested that the injuries on his body were likely caused by bamboo poles during the retrieval process. The most ridiculous thing was that a general affairs officer named Peng Changxia from Rugao disguised himself as a woman and fled after the incident, but was still captured. During the court hearing, he was still in women's clothing. After the interrogation, County Magistrate Chen stated that since the anti-narcotics division was established by provincial order, it was not appropriate to detain the acting director, Zhang Luxuan. The remaining personnel were placed under the custody of the Public Security Bureau, and the details of the case were telegraphed to the Civil Affairs Department of the provincial government for instructions.

Xiaoshan

Night Boat Robbed in West Xiaojiang 105

One night, in the Yangfan Mine area of West Xiaojiang, a night boat sailing from Shaoxing to Xixing was robbed by two bandit boats carrying over ten bandits. The over twenty passengers on the boat had all their luggage and money, totaling over one hundred yuan, searched and robbed. Fortunately, the boatmen worked hard to pull him out, preventing him from drowning.

Yesterday's Opium Suppression Commemoration 112

Anti-Drug Association Holds Meeting

Second Special Court Burns Opium

Yesterday was the 94th Opium Suppression Commemoration Day. In addition to publishing a declaration on the previous day, which was published in yesterday's newspaper, the Shanghai Chinese National Anti-Drug Association held a commemoration meeting in the afternoon. The Second Special Court also publicly burned opium to commemorate the day. The details of each event are recorded below:

Commemoration Meeting Held 113

The Chinese National Anti-Drug Association has always been determined to fundamentally eliminate drugs. However, due to environmental pressures this year, it has been unable to actively work. Yesterday, for the Opium Suppression Commemoration Day, the association originally planned to hold a grand anti-drug campaign in conjunction with all sectors of society, but the plan did not materialize. Instead, they only held a commemoration meeting at the association's headquarters. At 2:00 PM, the association's Secretary-General, Huang JiaHui, convened all staff members to hold a meeting, paying respects to the portrait of Lin WenZhong and speaking about Lin's burning of opium at Humen and the current state of the opium scourge in our country. The ceremony was simple and concluded at 3:00 PM.

Public Burning of Opium 114

The Second Special District Court of this city, in order to awaken public awareness on the Opium Suppression Commemoration Day, publicly burned a large amount of opium at 2:00 PM in the open space east of the court on Xuehuali Road. The opium burned included opium, opium paraphernalia, and other drugs such as morphine and heroin confiscated from January 4th to the end of March this year. The court's president, Ying Shi, personally supervised the event and invited representatives from various agencies and organizations to attend and observe. The Anti-Drug Association also sent Li Yunzeng as a representative to participate.

County Government Commemoration 115

Yesterday was the June 3rd Opium Suppression Commemoration Day. The Shanghai County Government held a commemoration meeting in the Great Hall at 10:00 AM. The entire staff of the Education Bureau, the Technology Office, and various departments of the County Government attended. County Magistrate Cao Zhenfei presided, Hu Gongshou recorded, and Ge Xiusheng served as the master of ceremonies. After the ceremony, the chairman reported the significance of the meeting and commemoration. Then, the Director of Education, Shi She, and others spoke about the various harms of opium. The ceremony concluded.

Gan Naiguang Discusses Local Autonomy in Various Provinces 116

Zhejiang Has the Best Results, Hubei and Jiangsu Are Next

Ministry of Interior Urges Provinces to Proceed

Gan Naiguang, the Vice Minister of the Interior, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday morning and returned to his private residence on Avenue Foch. Soon after, because the Minister of the Interior, Huang Shaoxiong, was about to go to Fujian, he visited Huang at his residence on Rue de l'Eglise to discuss departmental affairs for two hours before returning. A Central News Agency reporter visited him at his residence and asked about local autonomy and other matters. His remarks are recorded below:

Local Autonomy Achievements in Various Provinces 117

According to Gan, the importance of local autonomy is well known. Since the Ministry of the Interior took over the project, all provinces have earnestly complied. Although it has not yet been fully achieved, all provinces have made considerable progress. According to internal surveys, Zhejiang Province has achieved the best results in local autonomy, followed by Hubei. Jiangsu Province has made less progress due to various difficulties. Zhejiang Province has completed 70-80% of local autonomy. According to the laws and regulations promulgated by the central government, local areas in all provinces must complete local autonomy by 1934. Whether they can be completed as scheduled cannot be determined at this time.

Urging Provinces to Proceed 118

The scope of local autonomy includes sanitation, water conservancy, transportation, fisheries, animal husbandry, and mining area management. Therefore, the scope is very broad, and it is difficult to implement. The Ministry of the Interior can only uphold the central government's intentions and work hard to urge the provinces to proceed. As for the local autonomy pilot zone in Guangxi Province, the results of the survey are excellent. The Ministry of the Interior will also gradually implement local autonomy in Hunan and other provinces.

Rectifying Various Defense Corps 119

The various resolutions passed at the Second National Conference on Internal Affairs have been implemented one by one. The reorganization of local defense corps organizations has also begun. Local defense corps not only protect the local area but also promote the martial spirit of the Chinese people. Therefore, the reorganization of the corps is an urgent matter. It was also learned that Gan will return to Nanjing on Monday due to busy departmental affairs.

Shao Lizi Discusses the Shaanxi Disaster 120

Came to Shanghai Yesterday Morning to Negotiate Relief Funds

Returning to Nanjing Tonight, Going to Shaanxi on the 8th

Shao Lizi, the newly appointed Chairman of the Shaanxi Provincial Government, arrived in Shanghai by overnight train from Nanjing the night before last. He arrived at the North Station at around 8:00 AM yesterday morning and immediately returned to his residence to rest. A Central News Agency reporter visited Shao at his residence yesterday morning and asked about the recent situation in Shaanxi and the date of his assumption of office. He provided a detailed response as follows:

Shaanxi Disaster is Severe According to Shao, Shaanxi has suffered from droughts for many years. The disaster area is large, and there are many victims. Although various charitable organizations have repeatedly provided relief, it is a drop in the bucket and does not solve the problem. Recently, Shaanxi Province has received timely rain, hoping that this year's autumn harvest will be promising and the people's difficulties will be slightly alleviated. However, an unexpected event occurred. I recently received a telegram from Director Yang Hucheng stating that Shaanxi Province was hit by a wind disaster last month, and the wheat harvest is completely hopeless. The only way to provide relief at present is to replant. However, the farmers' seeds, tools, and livestock have long been lost. Although they have the desire to replant, they do not have the ability to do so. They can only look up at the sky and sigh, waiting to die. It is expected that this year's disaster will be even more severe than in previous years, and there will definitely be more victims than in previous years.

Planning for Relief Shao continued, "My biggest task in going to Shaanxi this time is to provide disaster relief. The reason why I have been delayed is that I am busy negotiating relief matters. The Central Party Headquarters previously allocated 20,000 yuan for disaster relief in Shaanxi, and has now decided to allocate another 50,000 yuan to purchase seeds for disaster relief. I have contacted various charitable organizations in Shanghai and asked them to provide relief. The charitable organizations also recognize the severity of the disaster in Shaanxi and are actively planning and trying to provide relief. The commissions earned from today's (3rd) Golden Goblet Champagne Race, which were originally intended to be used for disaster relief in Henan, Anhui, and Hubei provinces, have now been decided to be used in part for disaster relief in Shaanxi. However, the exact amount has not yet been determined.

Date of Assuming Office Shao is scheduled to take the overnight train to Nanjing tonight and go west to Shaanxi and Gansu on the 8th with Zhu Shaoliang, the Chairman of the Gansu Provincial Government, to assume their respective offices. Zhu took the overnight train to Nanjing last night to wait for Shao to travel together. Regarding the personnel for the various departments of the Shaanxi Provincial Government, Shao said that except for the directors of the Civil Affairs Department and the Finance Department, the rest will remain the same. There will be no changes. As for the candidates for the directors of the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments, they should be approved and announced by the Executive Yuan meeting next Tuesday.

He Bingxian Discusses the International Trade Bureau 121

He Bingxian, Director of the International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, took a leave of absence last month due to illness and was hospitalized for treatment. He has now fully recovered and returned to the bureau to handle affairs. According to Director He, the special bureau for trade with Russia has been thoroughly planned, but a decision can only be made after Minister of Finance Song Ziwen returns from Europe. Therefore, it is currently on hold. Our country's export trade to the Philippines has always been very developed. The Philippine industrial delegation came to China for sightseeing and to meet with various sectors of society, which will further promote the future of trade between the two countries. However, the nature of the delegation focuses on emotion, so although there have been talks, there have been no specific decisions.

Japanese Goods Dumped, China's Rubber Industry in Danger 123

Over Ten Factories Forced to Close

Workers Petition the Social Affairs Bureau for Relief

China's rubber industry has been developing since 1917, with new factories springing up one after another. However, in recent years, due to the impact of the current situation, it has only been able to maintain expenses. Recently, with the brisk sales of Japanese goods and the accumulation of inventory, it has become difficult for factories to maintain operations. Therefore, there has been a wave of closures, layoffs, and dismissals. According to Wan Yunfang of the Rubber Industry Association, there are 37 members of the association in the city, and four non-members. All of them are experiencing tight cash flow, inventory accumulation, and sluggish sales, resulting in one-third of them announcing closures. Based on the current situation, if sales do not improve, the rubber industry is likely to go bankrupt. The reason for this is that the industry's goods have traditionally been sold to the Northeast. Now, the Northeast market has been seized by Japan, and the products of local factories can only be sold in the upper and lower reaches of the Yangtze River. Because there are too many products, supply exceeds demand, making it impossible to maintain operations. The situation of each factory is recorded below:

Huatong Rubber Factory, Huatong Feihong Branch Road, has a total of 400 male and female workers. It has been open for almost four years. In the past, business was good. This year, due to the impact of the current situation, inventory cannot be sold. The factory shortened working hours from April 1st to avoid losses. On May 27th, it announced its closure. When workers inquired about the reopening date, the factory did not give a date, causing panic among all the workers. On May 31st, they negotiated with the factory but were rejected. Unable to do anything else, 40 representatives, including Xie Fulong, Chen Asan, Sun Chengkun, Yang Zhaonian, Qiu Genghui, Wu Youfu, and Zhu Jinbao, submitted a written petition to the Social Affairs Bureau at 9:00 AM yesterday, requesting a prompt resolution. Wu Xianqing, the director of the Mediation Section, received them and promised to send someone to investigate immediately. At 10:30 AM, Zhu Guilin from the Third Section of the Social Affairs Bureau went to investigate the truth.

Dade Rubber Factory, Gaolang Bridge, has a total of 50 male workers and 200 female workers. It announced its closure the day before yesterday (the 1st). All the workers immediately submitted a petition to the Social Affairs Bureau, requesting relief. The Social Affairs Bureau sent Zhu Guilin, a staff member from the Third Section, to mediate at 1:00 PM yesterday afternoon. A solution has been found.

Huashun Rubber Factory, Kangnaotuo Road, has a total of over 100 male and female workers. It announced its closure on April 9th due to various reasons. Although the Party and government agencies have mediated several times in the past two months, no solution has been reached due to differing opinions on both sides.

Minghua Rubber Factory, Dapuqiao, has a total of over 60 male and female workers. It announced its closure last year due to the impact of the war. As of now, it has not reopened due to tight cash flow.

Dayong Rubber Factory, Taopeng Road, has a total of over 400 male and female workers. It suspended all work from May 25th due to sluggish sales. No solution has been reached for a week.

Great China Welfare Rubber Factory, Xingjiazhai Road, has a total of over 300 workers. In February of this year, a strike dispute arose due to the dismissal of workers. The Social Affairs Bureau mediated several times, but no agreement was reached due to conflicting opinions. It has been three months, and no solution has been reached. It is reported that the factory and the workers are currently negotiating.

Dahua Rubber Factory, Meizhou Road, employs over 100 male and female workers. It announced its closure last year due to the accumulation of inventory and inability to sell it. It has been closed for half a year, and there is no reopening date.

Yiyuan Rubber Factory, North Chengdu Road, caused a strike dispute in March due to the unwarranted dismissal of workers. After mediation by the Party and government agencies, a temporary solution was reached. The dismissed workers, Cai Richu, Yang Yan, and Li Rong, will not return to work for the time being. Now, the Social Affairs Bureau has decided that workers Cai Richu and Yang Yan will be allowed to return to work, but the factory has refused. Unable to do anything else, workers Li Rong and Cai Richu submitted a written petition to the Social Affairs Bureau at 10:00 AM yesterday. Wang Xianqing, a staff member from the Third Section, received them and promised to send someone to mediate.

Dazhong Rubber Factory, New Jia坡 Road, the factory announced its closure on the 13th of last month. After mediation by the Party and government agencies, it was decided that the factory was unable to operate. The factory agreed to provide food, and the workers received 100 yuan at the end of last month to barely maintain themselves. Yesterday, they ran out of food and requested assistance from the Party and government agencies. The Social Affairs Bureau sent Tan Peiyan, a staff member from the Third Section, along with workers Shen Rongquan and Xu Yunjia to accompany them. The factory provided 100 yuan for food expenses.

Chinese Cotton Mills

Second Phase of Continued Work Reduction Yesterday 124

However, Shenxin, Tongyi, etc., Have All Canceled the Reduction

Fear of Cotton Shortage, Various Factories Seek Remedy

After the Hengfeng and other Chinese cotton mills continued to reduce work, yesterday was the second day of the reduced work period. However, the factories under Shenxin and others continued to work as usual. Various manufacturers are trying to find remedies. The details are recorded below:

Continued Work Reduction 125

Yesterday was the second phase of continued work reduction after the expiration of the first reduction period. In this city, a total of 28 factories, with 1,066,920 spindles, 9,060 thread spindles, and 7,864 looms, stopped working or continued to reduce work. There were 17 factories including Hengfeng. Factories that canceled the work reduction included 8 factories including Shenxin and Tongyi. The Jingwei and Chongxin factories have never reduced work. The workers in the closed factories live scattered in their homes, maintaining good order. They continued to stop working as usual today and will resume work tomorrow morning.

Fear of Cotton Shortage 126

The total amount of raw materials for textiles in this city, including domestic cotton, American cotton, and Indian cotton, is less than 400,000 dan. According to the needs of the Chinese and foreign cotton mills in the city, this is not enough to maintain operations for even one month. After the panic occurred before the new cotton was available, the Municipal Government and others discussed ways to rescue the Chinese cotton mills the day before yesterday, deciding to telegraph Minister Song in the United States for help. As for the Shanghai cotton mills, they have been trying to transport the cotton stored in the interior and producing areas to Shanghai to make up for the shortage and avoid shutdowns due to a lack of raw materials. Japanese Conspiracy to Seize Our Indigo Industry 128

Indigo Factories Close Down, Indigo Workers Lose Jobs

Indigo blue is the only essential element for dyes in our country. Japan has never manufactured indigo blue, but in recent years has been thinking of ways to seize our indigo industry. They even came up with a bizarre idea to use the residual sulfur black from their manufacture of explosives and dump it in China. In general unscrupulous merchants, are being fooled and are also acting insane, accepting and distributing it everywhere on their behalf. The application procedures for sulphur black and indigo blue are different. As soon as a dye shop adopts sulphur black, all the internal equipment must be completely changed. As a result, no fewer than thousands of domestic indigo dye factories have closed at the same time, and tens of thousands of dye workers have lost their jobs. Farmers who used to plant indigo as a profession have also stopped. The statistics are as follows and are specially disclosed to warn the commercial and industrial circles in our country. If we do not rise up and pursue the matter, our indigo industry will be completely seized by the Japanese.

Impose Anti-Dumping Duties

Review of the Nature of Dumped Goods 129

Establishment of a Committee to Review Dumped Goods

The US Will Also Levy Anti-Dumping Duties on Japanese Dumping

According to the Guowen News Agency, Japanese goods are being dumped in our country, attempting to counteract the impact of our boycott movement and significantly affecting the future of our domestic industries. The Ministries of Finance and Industry jointly proposed levying anti-dumping duties last month to protect the domestic goods market. A review committee has already been established. Simultaneously, the United Kingdom is also preparing for these tariff regulations due to the impact of Japanese dumping. Details are noted as follows:

Review Committee 130

The Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry, led by the Director-General of Customs, Shen Shuyu, together with the three directors of the Ministry of Industry's Commerce, Industry, and Agriculture departments, have organized a committee to review dumped goods. It has been established in the capital, and for convenience, an office has also been set up in this city, which has already started operating. The committee will begin by conducting reviews, strictly examining all imported goods to determine whether they are being dumped. Then, they will establish categories of dumped goods and implement taxes.

UK Suffers from Dumping 131

British colonies and their commercially monopolized markets, such as India, Burma, Persia, and Egypt, have recently also suffered from the harm of Japanese goods dumping, significantly impacting the British goods market. Therefore, the United Kingdom is adopting the same policy as our country, preparing to levy anti-dumping duties. Our authorities have already consulted with the UK regarding implementation methods to learn from their experience.

Reasons for Dumping 132

Yesterday, someone familiar with the current state of international economics stated that dumping policies are an inevitable result of overproduction. While levying anti-dumping duties is a remedial measure, the fundamental issue still lies in the recovery of global prosperity. Some manufacturers abroad, in light of the fact that ceasing or reducing production does not save on expenses but rather leads to unemployment for workers, implement dumping of light industrial products to safeguard the livelihoods of workers. Recently, on the market, vendors can be seen everywhere selling lightweight rubber balls shaped like balloons for only a few small coins. These goods are a type of dumped product, and so on.

Record of the Standing Committee Meeting of the Industrial and Commercial Management Association 134

Held for the 40th Time

Chen Baocheng's Speech

Yesterday, the China Industrial and Commercial Management Association convened its 40th standing committee meeting at the Lianhua General Association at No. 4 Beijing Road, gathering various industrial and commercial members. Representatives Wu Shizhao, Fang Yexian, Cheng Shouchong, Zeng Yunxiang, Zheng Yuanxing, Shao Zenghua, Ma Yanhua, and others, over 20 people in total, attended. In addition to reporting and discussing association affairs, to enable all members to understand the implementation of factory inspections, they specially invited Chen Baocheng of the International Labour Office to give a speech on "The Factory Law Implementation Problem in Concessions and Foreign Factories." Mr. Chen had done much research on this issue and spoke in great detail. A summary of his main points is as follows: Mr. Chen stated that the issue of factory inspection was a preliminary task after the National Government promulgated the Factory Law. At that time, the International Labour Office also participated in discussions, but due to the significance and complexity of the issue, although the results were close at the time, they were delayed for several years due to interruption and have not been implemented yet. Recently, the Municipal Council suddenly amended Article 34 of the Yangjingbang Regulations in the Westerners' Annual Meeting, with the aim of seizing our country's factory inspection rights. However, it still requires discussion by the Diplomatic Corps. If it is passed by the Diplomatic Corps in the future, the negotiations on factory inspection in the concessions will not have good results, so everyone should not neglect it. However, one must also not disregard the Factory Law because of factory inspections. The most important thing is to actively implement the provisions of the Factory Law to the best of one's ability to achieve excellent results, which can also be used as a basis for rejecting inspections in future negotiations. In short, we should recognize the purpose of the Factory Law and seek ways to implement it, so that the responsibilities of factories can be reduced, equal treatment for labor and management can be achieved, and considerable effectiveness can be obtained, which is also the only way to enhance government negotiations. Furthermore, to actively seek the improvement of factory management, the association recently dispatched personnel to inspect various major factories, aiming to achieve good factory management and obtain considerable results.

The two roads have established the Freight Rate Research Association to research the current freight rates in order to adapt to the environment and improve business. 2. The committee has one director and six members. In addition to the Director of the Traffic Department and the Head of the Business Section of the Traffic Department as ex officio members, the remaining members are appointed by the bureau director from among the staff of the two roads. 3. The committee members are unpaid and will not receive additional subsidies. 4. The committee holds a regular meeting once every two weeks, but special meetings may be convened when necessary. 5. When the committee meets, it may invite personnel from all levels of the Traffic Department or freight inspectors to attend for consultation. 6. The committee may request the bureau director to transfer assistant personnel from various departments when necessary. 7. All decisions made by the committee should be reported to the bureau director for adoption and implementation. 8. These regulations will take effect from the date of approval by the bureau director and will be submitted to the Ministry of Railways for record. 9. If there are any matters not covered by these regulations, they may be submitted to the bureau director for amendment at any time.

The Fisheries Improvement Committee of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang area, due to the collection of fisheries construction fees, at the beginning, all fisheries were able to appreciate the government's intention to construct fisheries, and all were happy to comply, such as various industries in Shanghai having already complied. Opening of the Sanjiangkou New Channel 144

Changjiang Wheel Boat Abandons the Tuanfeng Route

The inland waterways of the Yangtze River have been changing frequently in recent years. The Yangtze River Waterway Management Committee, as the upstream and downstream Yangtze River vessels have always had to travel around Tuanfeng when going above Anqing, the waterway is curved, and the voyage takes more than one and a half hours more. The Yangtze River Waterway Management Committee has started to open the Sanjiangkou route, covering more than 30 miles of river surface, with the water depth opened to 26-27 feet, so that even large ships of 4-5,000 tons can navigate. The Sanjiangkou route has already been opened, and the ships that travel in and out of the Yangtze River have already begun to take the Sanjiangkou route, abandoning the Tuanfeng route.
