Clever Plan to Sell Morphine 151

Wrapping Drugs in Newspapers

Sent from Chongqing to Shanghai by Mail

Wu Yulin, a Sichuan native, 48 years old, residing at No. 6, Gengyu Lane, No. 489 Rue Paul Beau, New Peace Apartments, Room 3, was selling morphine with Ji Xuanquan at No. 65 Quanxue Street, Chongqing, Sichuan, using more than ten names, including Wu Yongzhi, Wang Linsheng, Lin Xiasheng, Wu Yulin, Lin Xiasheng, Wu Yulin, Kong Xiang. The method was clever, and outsiders could not easily see through it. The secret was that Ji in Sichuan wrapped the drugs in newspapers and mailed them to Shanghai, addressed to Wu, or to Chen Xinfang and Li Quanan at the Shufeng Yin'er Company near the Daiteng Bridge on Avenue Edward VII and the Huiji Xing Customs Brokerage in Mantingfang, or to the Dahua Apartments on Rue Paul Beau, for Wu to receive and sell. The proceeds were sent to Sichuan. From the 8th to the 18th of last month, as many as 32 items (each item being a roll of newspaper) had been mailed to Shanghai, and Wu had made a considerable profit by selling them. This time, the Postal Bureau on Kai'er Road, Ba Xianqiao, received six rolls of newspapers from Ji Xuanquan in Chongqing, Sichuan, addressed to Wu, weighing 1,892 grams. Suspicious, they inspected them and discovered that the rolls were filled with drugs. They reported it to the police, and detectives Xu Desheng, Bao Tan Liu Jinrong, and Shen Jinshi rushed to New Peace Apartments at 4:00 PM the day before yesterday and arrested Wu, as well as Chen Xinfang and Li Quanan, who were involved. They also confiscated a bill of the 32 rolls of newspapers previously received at Wu's residence and took them to the police station for temporary detention. Yesterday, they were escorted to the Criminal Division 1 of the Second Special District Court. Judge Xiong interrogated them. Police lawyer Gu Shouxi stated the case, prosecuted under Article 6 of the Anti-Smoking Law, and requested a postponement for further investigation. He then presented the evidence. Detective Liu Jinrong reported the progress of the case and the arrest of the defendants. The defendants denied and quibbled. The court ordered a rescheduled hearing in ten days, and the defendants were remanded in custody.

Ten Years of Marriage, One Morning of Strife

Separation Followed by Lawsuit 153

Infatuated with a Prostitute, He Drives a Car to the Dance Hall

How Will Yang Yuqin Face His Wife?

Yang Yuqin, a cosmetics salesman who also works at Minli Middle School, is thirty-four years old. Ten years ago, he married a Miss Ding through a matchmaker. His wife is now thirty-three years old. The couple originally lived together at No. 67 Race Course Road and were initially very harmonious. Since last year, however, they suddenly developed animosity towards each other, turning affection into coldness. Yang refused to acknowledge Miss Ding as his wife, claiming that their union was never formal and that they might as well go their separate ways. Miss Ding, on the other hand, claimed that Yang, infatuated with Yang Lanchun from Qunyufang, intended to abandon his wife. They frequently quarreled and sometimes even resorted to violence. Last year alone, they were involved in lawsuits twice, both initiated by Miss Ding, first accusing him of abuse and insult, which was resolved through court mediation. Then, she sued him for neglecting to provide alimony, which was also mediated by the judge, who ordered the defendant, Yang Yuqin, to pay 60 yuan per month for living expenses and ordered the plaintiff, Miss Ding, to rent a separate residence, hoping that after a considerable period, their feelings would reconcile and they could reunite. However, Yang Yuqin had other intentions and disregarded the court mediation record as a mere formality, never paying the alimony as ordered, or only paying a small amount. Last month, Miss Ding petitioned the First Special District Court again, requesting immediate enforcement. At this time, Yang Yuqin filed a lawsuit against Miss Ding to terminate their relationship, because Yang denied that Miss Ding was his wife, he did not call it a divorce, but a termination of relationship. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Yang from the Civil Court of the court held a hearing. Yang Yuqin testified that he and Miss Ding were indeed only living together. After the court mediation last year, the defendant did not comply with the order to live separately and only recently moved out. Because he runs a cosmetics business, he needs to socialize. Occasionally, he goes to dance halls to dance with female friends, and she makes trouble on this pretext. He is truly suffering and cannot afford to pay alimony. He requests a clean break. Then, Miss Ding testified that she married him as his wife, with a marriage certificate and a matchmaker as proof, twelve years ago. He once said that the marriage certificate was forged by her, which is ridiculous. Now he wants to divorce her because he is having an affair with Yang Lanchun, so that he can live with his mistress. If he says he has no money, then how can he afford to drive a car, visit his mistress, and go to dance halls? She asked the court not to believe his lies. She would not consider divorce, nor would she consider reducing the amount of alimony. However, since the mediation, he has not paid a single month. She filed a petition for enforcement because she had no way to survive. She also presented a red marriage certificate as evidence. Judge Yang, after reviewing the evidence, stated that because the defendant disputed the issue of identity, further investigation was necessary. Therefore, he adjourned the hearing for a later date.

A Joke Leads to Disaster 158

An Apprentice Dies...A Worker is Injured

Yaohua Dyeing and Weaving Factory, located at No. 105 Caishi Road in the French Concession, prints and dyes various kinds of silk fabrics. It is a joint-stock company managed by Li Zhonghua from Haimen. There are over a hundred workers and apprentices. Yesterday, at 1 PM after lunch, a worker named Xie Jifang, 17 years old, from Haimen, was smoking a cigarette upstairs during his break. A fellow apprentice named Chen Pengnian, 20 years old, went up to joke with Xie and tried to stop him from smoking, snatching the cigarette and throwing it on the floor. Xie smiled and lightly slapped Chen's face. As he bent down to pick up the cigarette butt, Chen grabbed a rope and tried to tie Xie's hands to a pillar. The two began to playfully wrestle. Unexpectedly, as they wrestled near the staircase, they both lost their footing and fell down the stairs. Xie was in front and fell to the ground first, injuring both arms. Chen fell to the ground behind him, bleeding from his mouth and nose. He lost consciousness immediately due to a head injury. The rope he was holding was still in his hand. When the factory staff saw what had happened, they reported it to the Xiahfei police station, who sent detectives to investigate. They sent Chen to Renji Hospital for treatment, and took Xie to the police station. Under questioning by the police chief, Xie said that his arms were sore and he asked the police to send him to Renji Hospital. After a doctor bandaged his wounds, the police brought him back to the police station. Chen's brain injury was too severe and he died after being admitted to the hospital for about an hour. The hospital notified the police station, who sent detectives to transport the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch for autopsy, pending investigation by the court. The police chief ordered Xie to be detained pending further investigation.

New Title List of the Song Dynasty Tripitaka 161

The Shanghai recently reproduced Song dynasty Tripitaka Sutras are managed by the Shadow Printing Song Edition Tripitaka Association at No. 714 Weihaiwei Road. The original was published in the fourth year of the Shaoding era of Emperor Lizong of the Song Dynasty (1231 CE) by the Yan Sheng Yuan in Pingjiang Prefecture, Qisha, over 702 years ago. At that time, a Tripitaka Sutra Bureau was specially established with a very well organised structure, with positions such as chief officer, text comparator, proofreader, bureau chief, and director, all appointed by famous monks and nuns. The entire Sutra consists of 6,310 volumes. Its characters are ancient and elegant, and the carving is exquisite, making it a great contribution to Buddhist art. The careful collation, thorough annotations, comprehensive prefaces, and numerous records all make it far superior to other Sutras in terms of benefiting research and promoting culture. Currently, only one copy is preserved in the Wolong Temple in Shaanxi, making it a unique copy in the world. The Association sent personnel to compile and photograph the Sutra. Since a small number of volumes were corroded and blurred, they were supplemented with good copies sought from Beijing, Sichuan, Fujian, Guangdong, and other places (it is said that the supplemented copies are from the Sixi Edition, Puning Edition, Jingding Lu Daoyuan Edition, and Yanyou Yihmishi Edition). Only over 200 volumes.) The style of reproduction follows the original edition in every way, the number of lines and characters are the same, without any cutting. It is also very convenient for collecting, reciting and reading. The criticisms of this Sutra from all parties agree that its volumes are magnificent, its spirit is full, and there has never been a shadow of a Song edition book like this. Each pre-ordered copy is sold for only 525 yuan because the initiators wish for its circulation and do not consider it for commercial purposes at all. Before pre-orders are released, 60 to 70 copies have already been sold. Since advertisements were published in various newspapers, libraries, Buddhist temples, academic groups across the country, and universities in Europe, America, and Japan have sent letters and telegrams requesting samples. Due to economic constraints, the Association only printed 500 copies, which will not be enough to distribute. Furthermore, due to various reasons, the films (commonly known as wet films) cannot be re-printed in the future. Therefore, if you order a little later, you may regret not having it. The Association has investigated that the names of domestic customers who have paid the deposit up to May are listed as follows. Western and Eastern names have not been included: Two Dharma masters, Mo Chen Zhi Heng, one copy, Song Dezhong one copy, Zhou Shouliang one copy, Yang Zhonghu one copy, Penang Buddhist College one copy, Quantang Zhaoqing Temple one copy, Dharma master Xing Ci three copies, Di Chuqing seven copies, Kuai Ruomu one copy, Tian Yunshan one copy, Yuan Shaoming one copy, Yang Yuncun one copy, Ni Wenqing one copy, Ms. Li Xuying one copy, Dongfang Tuchun Hall one copy, Rong Desheng one copy, Ninja Grass Grove one copy, Baisha Brahma Temple one copy, Fentuoli Room one copy, Fayun Temple one copy, Li Qiqing one copy, Liu Huizhi one copy, Ji Mingyou one copy, Wu Haiuo one copy, Zhenjiang Library one copy, Nantong Library one copy, Kaifu Temple one copy, French Seminary one copy, Tang Shoupeng one copy, Shangfang Temple one copy, Zhou Zhian two copies, Lady Ho Tung two copies, Yongliwei Firm one copy, Hu Shaoqing one copy, Tsinghua University Library one copy, Ding Ziying one copy, Yao Wenfu one copy, Lingnan University Library one copy, Department of Affairs Printing Press one copy, Yu Kailing one copy, Ma Shaotang one copy, Dayu Buddhist Association one copy, Jueyuan Fa Bao two copies, Dharma master Yin Guang one copy, Huang Yi Qiu one copy, Chen Jingtao four copies, Guanghua University Library one copy, Zhao Yunchang one copy, Yunnan Provincial Government one copy, Qian Ziquan one copy.

Dies While Watching Airplanes 166

Zhang Quanrong, a white lead worker from Wuxi, was employed at the residence of Mr. Zhu at a certain number on Changsha Road, west of Zhang's Garden in the Public Concession. He was thirty-eight years old. Yesterday at around 5:45 PM, two airplanes were heard rumbling in the sky, approaching from afar. Zhang's curiosity was aroused, and he rushed to the drying platform, looking up into the sky. The handrail of the drying platform, due to years of disrepair, was severely corroded and snapped in two. As a result, Zhang lost his footing and fell. His skull was fractured, and he died immediately. After someone reported to the police station, the Xinzha Fire Brigade was notified, and an ambulance was dispatched to the scene. The body was transported to Renji Hospital and then to the autopsy center for examination.

China Merchants Bureau Still Has Unredeemed Shares 167

Special Deposit from the Central Bank

The Ministry of Communications, considering that the China Merchants Bureau still had remaining shares that had not been redeemed, specially ordered the Bureau's board of directors on the 3rd to handle the matter flexibly. After verifying the actual amount, each set would still be redeemed at 50 taels of silver. At the same time, an announcement would be made in the newspapers to inform the public.

Two Industries Appeal for the Return of Import Tax on Artificial Silk 168

Representatives Appointed from Silk Weaving and Silk Brocade Industries

The domestic trade of national silk brocade has been seized by Japanese goods. In recent years, sales have plummeted, to less than two or three out of ten. In addition, the price of silk in the domestic market has also been falling daily, making it difficult to maintain costs and resulting in excessive write-downs. The silk industry is facing bankruptcy and is in a precarious situation. Previously, the Electric Silk Weaving Factory Association and the Silk Brocade Industry Association of this city, recognizing the situation, decided to petition the government for the return of the import tax on rayon. They convened a meeting the day before yesterday and appointed representatives to go to Beijing to petition. The appointed petitioners from the associations include Wang Shiqiang, Gao Shiheng, Qian Boxi, Cai Xintao, and Huang Jiwen from the Electric Silk Weaving Factory Association, and Pan Runsheng and Zhang Hongsun from the Silk Brocade Industry Association. At the same time, they sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to appoint a representative to lead the two industries and assist in the petition. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce replied that the matter had been submitted to the 37th Standing Committee meeting for deliberation, and Standing Committee member Wang Yansong was appointed as the representative. He will travel to Beijing with the group to conduct the petition. It is said that the departure date of the petition group is scheduled for the night train to Beijing on the 5th of this month.

Grand German Circus 169

Coming to Shanghai Soon to Perform

The world-renowned German Karl Hagenbeck Circus is currently performing in Japan. It is expected that the entire troupe will arrive in Shanghai in early September and will perform amazing stunts on the vacant lot of the former Dahua Hotel site, creating an unprecedented spectacle in Shanghai. Hagenbeck is the owner of the Stellingen Zoo near Hamburg, Germany, and has long been known worldwide. His zoo collects rare and exotic animals from all over the world. Since Hagenbeck led the entire troupe of actors and animal performers to Japan, it has been two months, and the audience has been packed every day. The wonder and astonishment of the performances are self-evident. The troupe employs many world-renowned circus experts. Apart from those with extremely high salaries, there are about 300 people. The total number of staff members is close to 1,000. The animals they bring include 100 horses of various sizes, as well as lions, tigers, bears, wolves, deer, elephants, giraffes, rhinoceroses, camels, seals, and various other tame wild animals that accompany the troupe and are available for viewing. In recent years, there have been Western circuses coming to Shanghai, but none have been as grand as the Hagenbeck Circus this time. They will be performing in Shanghai for six weeks, which is unseen by the public and a visual feast.

Manager of the Jital Pawnshop in Taicang Embezzles 300,000 Yuan and Flees to Shanghai 170

Taicang Detectives Come to Shanghai to Arrest

The Jital Pawnshop in Taicang County has been established for over a hundred years and has a considerable reputation in the local area. Therefore, it absorbs a lot of deposits. The manager position was held by Gu Shouxian from Suzhou. Gu was known for his long sleeves and good dancing skills and had extensive connections. Unexpectedly, in recent years, he had a sudden thought of engaging in private malpractices, unilaterally embezzling funds from the pawnshop. If it was not enough, he would use the name of Jital to smooth things over with local banks. Over time, he embezzled as much as 300,000 yuan. Because his own pockets were full, Gu abandoned his post and fled with his loot, hiding at No. 520 Dagu Road in Shanghai. He lived a carefree life and traveled to foreign venues. Little did he know that extreme joy breeds sorrow, and that a cunning rabbit with three burrows had already been discovered by the Taicang County government. Because Gu was a wanted criminal who had fled after embezzling funds, it was unacceptable for him to escape again. Yesterday, they urgently reported to the Xinzha police station and requested assistance in the arrest. The police chief added Chinese and Western detectives to rush to the address, arrest Gu Shouxian, and escort him to the First Special District Court yesterday morning. Judge Qian Wenji interrogated the police station's lawyer Li Zhishan, who explained the case. Judge Qian then interrogated Gu. The Taicang County government had not yet formally delivered documents to the court for extradition, so it was ordered that Gu remain in custody for seven days, pending the arrival of the documents for extradition and further investigation.

Zhao Ruquan No Misconduct

Two Types of Conclusive Evidence Found by the Police 171

丨Yesterday's Continued Interrogation of Zhao Jiaobao's Release on Bail丨

The Sanxing Stage on Niuzhuang Road was established as a joint venture by actors Zhao Ruquan, Du Wenlin, Mao Yunke, Xie Yuekui, Jia Biyun, and businessman Zhou Bingchen, with Zhou serving as the front-of-house manager and Xie as the backstage manager. However, because Zhao Ruquan was quite familiar with the theater's operations, all the shareholders elected Zhao to manage the finances. Recently, Zhou Bingchen discovered evidence of Zhao's embezzlement, amounting to over 30,000 yuan. He reported this to the Zhabei Police Station and requested an arrest warrant from the First Special Court. On the night of the 29th of last month, at 12:30 AM, Chinese Detective Chen Yonggui, Sergeant Yang Guanying, and Foreign Detective Hui Tuo went to the backstage of the Sanxing Stage, arrested Zhao, and handed him over to the First Special Court for interrogation and detention.

Yesterday morning, Judge Feng Shide opened the court for continued interrogation. Zhou Bingchen hired lawyers Chen Rui, Du Jimei, and Yuan Yang'an to represent him, while Zhao Ruquan hired lawyers Jiang Yiping, Liu Shichao, and Shi Dubi to defend him. First, Police Officer Ru Baoyi stated that the police had found two types of conclusive evidence, totaling 1,214 yuan: 1) Advertising fees paid by the Lianshang Advertising Company to Zhao Ruquan, which Zhao received but did not record in the accounts; 2) Monthly interest of 10 taels from the 2,000 tael deposit at the Sheng Yi Electric Power Company, which Zhao also pocketed without recording it in the accounts. Zhao Zuwei, Zhao's accountant, is currently auditing the accounts and will report on them. The police have summoned Ma Zhongmou, Fu Guangting, and Liu Xianting, the three individuals from the Lianshang Company who paid the money to Zhao, and request that they be questioned.

Next, Zhou Bingchen submitted a statement claiming that on the "red ledger" copied and distributed by the defendant, only six yuan in advertising fees were recorded, which he discovered was not the actual amount. Furthermore, the capital of 21,000 yuan and the 10,000 yuan deposit were not indicated as being deposited in a money house, nor was there any interest from the money house. The matter is currently under investigation. Subsequently, Ma, Fu, and Liu testified that they handed the money to Zhao, totaling 1,250 yuan.

When asked, the defendant Zhao Ruquan claimed that regarding the advertising fees, because the contract was not yet fulfilled, he had stated to the shareholders at the end of last year that the distribution would be temporarily postponed. With the consent of the shareholders, he deposited the money in the Siming Bank and submitted a deposit book, as well as three other deposit books and eight packets of silver, and three accounting books to prove his impartiality. Witnesses Du Wenlin and Mao Yunke testified that Zhao had indeed stated about the advertising fees, but they could not confirm whether Zhou Bingchen was present at the time. Xu Junfu, the bookkeeper, also testified regarding the opening of the "red ledger" and that the advertising fee was not entered in the "red ledger" because the contract had not yet been fulfilled.

Police Officer Ru immediately stated that the police were currently investigating Xu for alleged collusion and embezzlement. After approximately three hours of proceedings, the court adjourned due to the late hour and announced that the hearing would resume next Friday afternoon. Lawyer Jiang immediately requested that Zhao be released on bail, but Lawyer Ru opposed this. The court stated that it would wait for the defendant to submit a written request to the court before making a decision. In the afternoon, Zhao submitted a written request to the court and was released on bail.

Shops Fined for Not Affixing Revenue Stamps 173

On May 29th, the Shanghai Second Special District Court heard a case involving violations of the Revenue Stamp Regulations. The three defendants, all businesses, were accused of using disguised invoices, establishing nominal items, evading stamp duties, or affixing an insufficient number of stamps. After a brief interrogation by the court's judge, all admitted to failing to affix the correct number of stamps. The Rongyang Hosiery Factory was fined 30 yuan, the He Sugar Company was fined 10 yuan, and the Meihuali Factory was fined 25 yuan as a warning.

Customs Notice Regarding Wool Export Tax Rate 175

Tang Haian, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and Tax Commissioner Bolade jointly issued a notice yesterday stating that, in accordance with government orders, starting from May 31st of this year, all shipments of waste wool (i.e., tangled wool from the head, abdomen, and legs of sheep) exported abroad, valued at no more than 15 yuan per dan (approximately 50 kilograms), will be taxed according to item No. 190 of the export tariff. All merchants are hereby notified.

Social Affairs Bureau Orders Tobacco Shops to Abide by Industry Regulations 176

The Shanghai Tobacco Trade Association previously proposed measures to address the chaotic pricing among its members and requested the relevant authorities to issue a strict prohibition. Yesterday, the association received a reply from the Social Affairs Bureau with order number 10228, stating that it had received a request to prohibit price chaos. The bureau noted that if members were indeed disrupting industry regulations and offering discounted prices, the association should, in accordance with Article 10 of the industry regulations, discuss and decide on punishment and sanctions and submit them for review. The request to issue a public notice was deemed unnecessary for the time being.

Executive Committee of the Chinese and Foreign Grocery Trade Association 177

The Shanghai Chinese and Foreign Grocery Trade Association, recognizing that the industry has suffered greatly in recent years due to the influence of the current situation, held its tenth executive committee meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday to devise ways to maintain the industry's business. Committee members Zhang Heshun, Peng Binghua, Cao Feng, Fang Xiaozhi, Cheng Yujie, and Wang Pingyuan, along with Chairman Cheng Yujie and Secretary Fu Keming, attended. Secretary Fu Keming reported on the resolutions of the previous meeting and correspondence. The resolutions were as follows:

(A) A letter from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce regarding the scheduled annual meeting of member representatives, requesting nominations for representatives and the submission of proposals. Cheng Yujie was nominated as the chairman's representative, and the following proposals were drafted: 1) Request the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce to promptly find ways to recover non-Japanese goods wrongly confiscated by the former Anti-Japanese Association to demonstrate good faith and protect capital. 2) The proposal to compel all members to join the association should be resubmitted to the government for swift approval to comply with laws and strengthen unity. The resolutions were passed.

(B) A letter from the Restaurant Association opposing the increase in telephone rates in the Chinese district and seeking opinions. Resolved: Approved in principle.

(C) Omitted.

(D) The Secretariat's draft industry regulations for review. Resolved: Approved with amendments and to be submitted to the members' meeting for discussion.

(E) Ratification of the resolutions of the fourth standing committee meeting. Resolved: Approved.

Committee member Cheng Yujie proposed a temporary motion that, in light of the recent impact of the current situation on the industry and the decline in business, to maintain business, the prices of goods should be increased, and one percent of the industry's business revenue should be set aside as a reserve fund, following the example of the banking industry, to prepare for and maintain business. Committee member Cao Yi seconded the motion. Resolved: Approved in principle. The detailed implementation plan will be submitted to the members' meeting for discussion.

Also, Committee member Cheng Yujie proposed that, in accordance with the association's articles of association, the annual meeting of member representatives should be held regularly. Committee member Wang Pingyuan seconded the motion. Resolved: To be held at the association's premises at 2:00 PM on July 1st (Saturday). The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Reader's Question

Why Complain and Blame Others? 189

A Letter from Mr. Wan, Jinan

Since I was young, I have been standing on the ugly and sordid side of society. To go a step further, the bad phenomena of the human world pour into my fragile brain every day. Unfortunately, my family is also declining day by day. My mother's gradually becoming thinner and more gloomy has deeply affected my inner self. So, I lost my vitality and courage. When I encountered external pressure, I could only fight back with patience and pain. As a result, a root of suspicion and fear was established in my inner self. Unfortunately, the banditry, which many people compare to floods and wild beasts, tore apart my already devastated family. My mother became a victim of this great calamity! My grandmother is temporarily living in the home of relatives in her hometown, and my wife is living in her maiden home. I am like a small boat floating in the vast sea. Today, I am tied to the side of this lonely island. Perhaps the wind will rise at night, and when I wake up tomorrow morning, I will be in another place! Not sinking is the ultimate happiness. I have not read many books. I have no specialized knowledge. Although I have spent several years in the ivory tower (here, the ivory tower is likened to a school, and it is a secondary school).

The introduction is over. I am sorry that I can only give you a faint impression!

As for human beings, except for innocent children, whether male or female, I dare not deeply believe that their hearts are pure and their thoughts are honest, especially the modern Chinese bureaucrats, politicians, and the X sticks that many people scold.

To society, I always feel that it is a deep black pool, or rather, it is a dung cellar. Everywhere there is only ugliness and stench.

Narrowing the scope a little, I feel only despair for China. Because I am convinced that the hearts of the Chinese people are selfish to the extreme. They have no sense of shame, no sense of love, especially like to play petty tricks, love to bully the weak, fawn over the strong, love to talk big, but do not love to do a small thing in reality. I feel only despair for such a nation. Even a glimmer of hope has been extinguished. Sometimes I think: If there is a person in front of me who can truly be not despicable and tricky at all, and has only a passionate heart, a heart to love all people, and a heart to help all people, then I would definitely fall into his arms and cry bitterly to thank him for giving me an ideal true human being.

In short, my eyes seem to be covered with a layer of dark web.

My inner self, at this moment, has the strongest demand: "How can I contribute my personal strength to society and to the people?" Because at this moment, I am still playing the role of a small clerk and I still do not have a real occupation.

I have thought about (and I am still thinking about it), it would be best if I could apply for some kind of reclamation department somewhere, and after graduation, go to the northwestern frontier, which is close to primitive humans. There, I can cultivate the land myself and forget everything in the past and start another life of joy.

I wrote in a chaotic and incoherent way. Let me sort out my questions!

1. Are society and humanity ugly and sordid, or not? Is my understanding of society and humanity comprehensive or one-sided?

2. Is life happy or painful? What methods should be used to obtain happiness?

3. What should be the criteria for seeking a job? What are the most beneficial jobs for society and the people at present?

These questions may not be worth asking, but they are some of the pains that I am anxious to solve. Gentlemen, please focus on this point and give me a troublesome answer!

In addition to the answers, if you can introduce some books that can be prescribed to the symptoms and call me to buy and read them, so that I can get a thorough solution, that would be the best. (Reply will be published tomorrow)

Zhejiang Province Secondary School Graduation Examination Date 190

Held in districts starting July 1

Decided and ordered by the Education Department to be informed

The date of the Zhejiang Province Secondary School Graduation Examination for the second semester of this year has been decided by the Education Department and ordered to be notified to all public and private secondary schools in the province. The dates are as follows:

A. June 28: Deadline for students to register for the graduation examination. B. July 1-3: Graduation examination held in districts. C. July 4-16: Grading and scoring of papers. D. July 17: Official announcement of results. E. July 20, 21, 22, 23: Re-examination in districts. F. July 22 - August 1: Grading and scoring of re-examination papers. G. August 2: Announcement of re-examination results. (Attached: Dates for enrollment in senior and junior high schools.) August 5 - 24: All schools must complete enrollment procedures during this period and must not delay beyond August 24. Remarks: 1. If there are any unforeseen obstacles that prevent the examination from being held on time, a separate announcement will be made at any time. 2. All schools should follow the dates prescribed by the secondary school regulations of the 21st year and hold the graduation examination in their respective schools. It is not allowed to advance or postpone the examination. The procedures for students participating in the graduation examination should be handled promptly.

Solicitation of Extracurricular Activity Photos from Students 192

(Nanjing, 3rd dispatch) The Ministry of Education approved a letter from the Central News Commission's Propaganda Committee. In order to collect materials on the development of education in our country to produce films or photographs as foreign propaganda materials, the ministry ordered all departments and bureaus to instruct the middle and primary schools under their jurisdiction to select the best works or photos of students' handicrafts, extracurricular activities, and vocational activities and send them to the minister for forwarding.

Teacher's Day on the 6th of this Month in This City 193

丨This City Will Hold Grand Celebrations丨

Second Preparatory Meeting of Municipal School Teachers and Staff

All Schools Participating Will Have an Afternoon Holiday

Gu Yinqian and Two Others Elected as Chairmen

Yesterday evening, the teachers and staff of the municipal primary schools in the Shanghai, Hùnán, Zháběi districts held their second preparatory meeting for the Teacher's Day celebration at Wànzhú Primary School. Representatives from 22 schools, including Wànzhú, Jìngyè, Xīchéng, Wùběn, Yǒngxīng, Yǎngzhèng, and Méixī, attended. Qián Xuǎnqīng was elected as chairman and Jiāng Mènglín as recorder. The meeting was conducted according to protocol. First, the chairman announced the purpose of the meeting and the significance of the celebration. Then, Hú Huáitiān reported that he had contacted the Education Bureau and had been granted permission for a half-day suspension of classes on the afternoon of Teacher's Day. The following resolutions were then discussed and decided upon: ㈠ The entire staff of the municipal primary schools in the Hùnán and Zháběi districts will hold a commemorative meeting at Yǎngzhèng Primary School at 1:30 PM on the 6th. Gù Yīnqián and Qián Cìjiǔ were appointed to convene the meeting. ㈡ All schools should fly flags on that day. ㈢ Director and section chiefs from the Education Bureau, supervisors, and Mr. Liú Hóngēn, Liào Shìchéng, and Zhèng Tōnghé were invited to give speeches. ㈣ Xú Jiǒngqiān and Hú Huáitiān were appointed to draft the declaration for the general meeting. ㈤ Zhāng Yǒngchūn was appointed to solicit commemorative writings for Teacher's Day celebrations. ㈥ Zhào Lǚqīng, Qián Xuǎnqīng, and Zhāng Yǒngchūn were appointed to the presidium of the general meeting. ㈩ Yáng Sòngyú and Qián Cìjiǔ were appointed to solicit performances by teachers and students from various schools. ㈧ At 6 PM that evening, a thank-you dinner will be held at the Dàfù restaurant, with the cost collected by Gù Yīnqián and Wáng Dìngchéng.

Health Education Exhibition Closed Yesterday 194

Exhibits Must Be Retrieved Before Noon Today

Yín Rúzhēn from Shàngwén Won First Place in the Dental Competition

The first Health Education Exhibition in the Southern District of the city closed yesterday at 5 PM. Hé'ān Primary School and the China Women's Physical Education School both gave outstanding performances. The finals of the dental health competition were announced yesterday, and awards were presented. Details are recorded below:

Notice from the Municipal Education Bureau Regarding the Retrieval of Exhibits to All Schools and Organizations Participating in the Exhibition: The Health Education Exhibition was held from June 1st to June 3rd and closed upon expiration. The borrowed venue should be returned immediately. All exhibits from all organizations and schools must be retrieved from the venue after 5 PM on June 3rd and before 12 PM on June 4th. Those exhibits from the schools that are marked with colored pen circles on the labels, exhibit catalogs, etc., will be retained by this bureau for permanent display or as materials for the Health Department to compile and print special publications. This is a special notice.

Award Ceremony for the Dental Competition: The finals of the dental health competition were held yesterday. The award ceremony was held at 4:15 PM in the lecture hall, presided over by Wú Lìguó, head of the School Health Section of the Health Bureau. Yín Rúzhēn (female), 14 years old, from Shàngwén Primary School, won first place and received 24 prizes. Qín Chéngkāng, 13 years old, from the First Charity Primary School, won second place and received 12 prizes. Cáo Róngmíng, 6 years old, from Pǔyìshè Kindergarten, won third place and received 8 prizes. The dentists were Sū Jiéláng and Huáng Réndé.

The Shanghai International Games Opened Yesterday

Confidence in the Chinese Championship 199

Our Country Sets a New National Record in the 400m Relay

The American Women's Championship is Guaranteed, with Outstanding Results

All Finals Today Afternoon 200

This year's Shanghai International Games opened yesterday at the China Athletic Field. Athletes from nine countries gathered to compete in men's and women's events. The elite were assembled, and the results were excellent. Over a thousand spectators attended, showing great interest. Wang Zhengting, Honorary Chairman of the Games, and Mayor Wu, Honorary President, both personally attended the opening ceremony. The competition results were particularly outstanding. In the 400m relay, our country's Huáng Fēilóng, Dǒng Yínchū, Wáng Jìlín, and Chéng Jīnguàn set a new national record of 46 seconds flat, breaking the previous record of 46.6 seconds held by the Beiping team. However, this was still far from the Games record of 44.8 seconds (created by the Americans). In addition, Xue Puhan's (English) 52.1 seconds in the 400m preliminary, Ms. Bai Naide's long jump of 4.875 meters, high jump of 1.405 meters, 100m of 13.4 seconds, and the American women's team's 55 seconds in the 400m relay all exceeded our country's highest records. As for the championship situation, our country has the best chance in the men's events, having already scored 32 points yesterday. The United States is second with 11 points. In the women's events, the United States is guaranteed the championship. All finals will be held today. Special results will appear one after another. Hopefully, our country's athletes will not be content with winning championships but will strive for special achievements. Our country's highest records must not be broken by athletes from other countries but must be surpassed by ourselves. We must not allow athletes from other countries to take all the glory. It should be known that our country's athletes are the elite of the nation. Now, competing with overseas Chinese and foreign athletes in Shanghai, they should rightfully win. The creation of new records is what we expect. Strive, strive!

A Group Photo of Chinese Male and Female Athletes (Photo by Lǐ Zūnyōng)

Opening Ceremony 201

A gentle breeze brushed the faces as they circled the venue, with thin clouds covering the sky. The athletes from nine countries entered the venue one after another. After a while, the McGinnis military band in front of the podium began to play, the music melodious and uplifting, majestic and stirring. Soon, the announcer stepped onto the stage and ordered the athletes from each country to enter in order and parade around the field. The military band led the way, followed by the staff. Next were the Chinese female athletes, followed by the American and British teams. Then, they were arranged according to the number of athletes, with the Chinese athletes last, showing their humility and hospitality. The athletes' uniforms were neat and their steps were synchronized, making it a spectacular sight.

Mayor's Speech After circling the field once, all the athletes faced the podium, and Honorary President Mayor Wu stepped onto the stage to deliver a speech, which was translated by Shěn Sìliáng. He briefly stated that the annual Shanghai International Games has arrived again. Looking back at the spirit and achievements of previous sessions, they have indeed improved with each passing day, which is a gratifying thing. As transportation has become increasingly convenient, the concept of segregation among human races has been abolished at an early date. Shanghai, as an important place for international gatherings, has greatly benefited from the International Games in terms of international friendship. We sincerely hope that all athletes will improve their performance in the future, and that international friendship will also progress with it.

(Right) First in High Jump (Middle) Wú Jǐnqí (Left) First in Long Jump (Middle) Wáng Jìhuái (Photos by Xú Tiānzhāng and Jiǎng Sōnglíng)

White Doves Flying: At the opening of the Olympic Games, white doves are often released, sometimes in the thousands, to symbolize peace. This time, the Shanghai International Games also followed this example, with over sixty carrier pigeons packed in three cages and brought to the venue. Colored paper strips were tied to the tails of the pigeons in advance. As soon as Mayor Wu finished speaking, the three cages were released simultaneously. Each pigeon trailed colored paper as it soared into the sky, looking from afar like long-tailed phoenixes of the nine heavens, truly a spectacular sight.

Beginning of the Games: Then, with the audience cheering and applauding, Honorary Chairman Wang Zhengting announced the beginning of the Games. The warriors entered the field, waiting quietly for the order to display their talents, and the air suddenly became tense.

Games Announcement 204

The prizes for the Games will be awarded immediately after the conclusion of each final. Prizes for yesterday's finals will be awarded today.

All members of the Chinese team and participating teams are requested to gather at the Association Building at 11:00 AM for lunch together. Latecomers will not be waited for.

Dai Ji, Commander of the Songhu Garrison, has generously donated two silver cups, one to be awarded to the winning country in the team competition and one to be awarded to the individual with the best performance.

Overview of Field Events 205

The field event finals included three men's events and two women's events. Wáng Jìhuái's long jump of 6.705 meters almost broke Pān Zuòxīn's national record of 6.74 meters and was the most satisfying result for Chinese athletes yesterday. As for the women's events, they were all won by American women. Bái Nàidè's outstanding records were awe-inspiring. A brief description is given below:

㈠ Unexpected Disappointment in the Discus 206

The discus was won by the Russian Mìluònuòfū in the previous Games with a throw of 35.42 meters, breaking his own record of 34.89 meters. The Chinese athletes participating included three generals: Lěng Péigēn, Gōng Wànyù, and Chén Bǎoqíu. In the first three throws, Lěng Péigēn was in first place with 34.45 meters. Unexpectedly, in the last three throws, Mìluònuòfū surpassed him in the sixth throw with 35.42 meters. Judging from this result, all three of Lěng, Gōng, and Chén have repeatedly exceeded this number on weekdays. Lěng regressed, and Gōng and Chén both failed to qualify. Gōng only managed 33 meters, and Chén managed 32 meters. It was a truly unexpected defeat. The scores of the four people are as follows:

First: Mìluònuòfū (Russia) 35.42 meters (New Games Record)

Second: Lěng Péigēn (China) 34.45 meters

Third: Huáwéikè (United States) 33.49 meters

Fourth: Mòtuōfūjīn (Russia) 33.49 meters

Appendix: Fifth: Fúlāsāi (England) 31.84 meters

Appendix: Sixth: Huìwéigè (Latvia) 31.84 meters

㈡ Wáng Jìhuái's Long Jump Masterpiece 207

Wáng Jìhuái won the long jump with 6.705 meters, just 0.035 meters short of the national record. It is said that Wáng once took a step backwards during this jump, otherwise,

He would have exceeded Pān Zuòxīn's record. During the fifth jump, Wang also had an excellent attempt, but it was invalidated for stepping over the board by half an inch, which was a pity. This was one of the most outstanding events for Chinese athletes yesterday. In the first three jumps, Wang was first, Wú Jǐnqí was second, and Chén Bǎoqíu was third. The Japanese, Xiǎosōng, was fourth, and the American, Shǐ Huángkè, was fifth. The Japanese, Gāng, was sixth. Unexpectedly, in the last, sixth jump, Xiǎosōng suddenly surpassed Wú Jǐnqí with 6.65 meters, and Gāng surpassed Shǐ Huángkè and Chén Bǎoqíu with 6.54 meters. The results of the six people are as follows:

First: Wáng Jìhuái (China) 6.705 meters (New Games Record)

Second: Xiǎosōng (Japan) 6.65 meters (New Games Record)

Third: Wú Jǐnqí (China) 6.61 meters (New Games Record)

Fourth: Gāng (Japan) 6.54 meters (New Games Record)

Appendix: Fifth: Shǐ Huángkè (United States) 6.51 meters (New Games Record)

Appendix: Sixth: Chén Bǎoqíu (China) 6.21 meters

㈢ The Chinese Team Dominates the High Jump 208

Yesterday's high jump was the most successful event for the Chinese team, taking the top three spots. Wú Jǐnqí's winning jump of 1.73 meters can also be considered a rare achievement. It is said that Gù's performance was equal to that of Chén Líng. Gù came second, one place behind Wu. Fourth place went to Huìwéigè of Latvia. The Chinese team scored an additional ten points in this event, greatly increasing their position for the championship.

㈣ Bái Nàidè's Astonishing Results 209

In the women's long jump, American Bái Nàidè narrowly lost to Zhuāng Míngzhēn last year by 0.01 meters. This year, she unexpectedly created a result of 4.875 meters, with her rapid progress being impressive. Tāngmǔshēng came second with 4.86 meters. This kind of record is unimaginable for Chinese women. Chén Shūqīng and Chén Róngmíng came third and fourth. Both Bái and Tāng broke the Chinese record. The results are as follows:

First: Bái Nàidè (United States) 4.875 meters (New Games Record)

Second: Tāngmǔshēng (England) 4.86 meters (New Games Record)

Third: Chén Shūqīng (China) 4.47 meters

Fourth: Chén Róngmíng (China) 4.43 meters

Appendix: Fifth: Qián Hángsù (China) 4.37 meters

In the high jump, this event was entirely dominated by blue-eyed, blond-haired people. Chinese women are far from being able to compete, with a significant difference in performance. The top three all exceeded the Chinese national record by a large margin. Bái Nàidè won with 1.405 meters, which is also an unimaginable result for Chinese women. Second place, Bào'ěr, had the same result as Bái Nàidè, but voluntarily gave up second place. Englishman Tāngmǔshēng was third, and American Tuōtuō'ěr was fourth. Such results for women are truly astonishing.

Track Finals 210

In the 1500 meters, twenty people participated. Our country's Dǒng Shūzhāo took the lead from the start, with Englishman Huálín and American Sāiwéisī following behind. After two laps, Sāiwéisī moved ahead, and Kèlèigé and Méngsī accelerated, competing fiercely for the lead. In the last hundred meters, Dǒng Shūzhāo and Sāiwéisī were neck and neck. Kèlèigé greatly increased his speed, beating Sāiwéisī by a shoulder at the finish line. The time was four minutes and twenty-five seconds. Dǒng Shūzhāo was third, and Méngsī was fourth, all with very little difference.

The previous champion in the men's relay was the United States. China was determined to take revenge. This time, with a wealth of talent, the hopes were naturally high. From the beginning, everything went smoothly. The first runner, Huáng Fēilóng, was ahead by a step. The second runner, Dǒng Yínchū, was extremely agile. The third runner, Wáng Jìhuái, sprinted very effectively. The fourth runner, Chéng Jīnguàn, led the pack and secured first place with a time of 46 seconds, setting a new national record for our country and breaking the previous national record of 46.6 seconds held by Beiping. The United States was second, far behind. Japan was third, and England was fourth. The lineup was as follows:

Team First Runner Second Runner Third Runner Fourth Runner ㈠ China Huáng Fēilóng Dǒng Yínchū Wáng Jìhuái Chéng Jīnguàn ㈡ United States Lāsīmòshēng Tāng Shǐlái Qù Fúyēlā Xǔ ㈢ Japan Gāngběn Qímù Xiǎosōng Gāng ㈣ England Mǎlín Màikègāo Kèlèigé Xuě Pūhàn

There were three countries in the women's relay. Our country's relay technique was not quick and sharp enough, resulting in third place. The American team won the championship with a time of 55 seconds, breaking the previous record of 57.8 seconds. England hesitated during the final leg, causing them to fall behind. Otherwise, they could have competed with the United States for the championship. The Chinese women were always in last place. The lineup of each country is as follows:

Team First Runner Second Runner Third Runner Fourth Runner ㈠ United States Bào'ěr Pōlín Sī Tuōtuō'ěr Bái Nàidè ㈢ England Tuōmǔshēng Bólóufēióutè Láilā Bó'ēn ㈡ China Qián Hángsù Chén Róngmíng Dǒng Jiéyīng Chén Shūqīng

Preliminary and Quarterfinal Rounds Report 221

Men's 100 Meters Begins: The first event was the Men's 100 Meters Preliminary Round, divided into four groups, with the top three from each group advancing. In the first group, the American, Yellach, was the fastest with 11.2 seconds, followed by Japan's Oka in second, and Germany's Parker in third. The competition was fierce. Unfortunately, China's Wang Jihuai encountered a strong group, fought hard but finished fourth, and was eliminated. The first place finishers in the following three groups were all Chinese athletes, but their times were not good. The American star Tom Slay lost to Cheng Jinguan, and Russia's Tomshas Gai fell. After the preliminary round, there was a ten-minute break before the quarterfinals. Yellach again won the championship, with Oka still behind Yellach. Huang Feilong fought hard to get third, with a time of 11.7 seconds, much slower than the preliminary round. In the second group, Cheng Jinguan also took first place with a time of 11.4 seconds, better than in the preliminary round. Chen Jiayou was not selected.

Women's 50 Meters Second Event Preliminary Round: The second event was the Women's 50 Meters. The American girl, White, is a famous star in this event, and the British Thompson is also not a weak contender. The two had a fierce competition. Qian Hangsu was third, and Sheng Bi was fourth and did not advance. White achieved the best time of 7.2 seconds. In the second group, the American Powell took first, and Chen Shuqing and Chen Baoxiang took second and third. It is likely that the champion and runner-up in the final will not be from China.

Men's 200 Meters, Four Groups Preliminary Round: The British Shepperd Han was the fastest with 23.5 seconds, followed by the American Yellach with 23.6 seconds in second. The Japanese Little Oka encountered Yellach in both the 100-meter preliminary and quarterfinal rounds. He met Yellach again in the 200 meters. Oka was defeated each time. Huang Feilong and Cheng Jinguan performed reasonably well. Dong Yinchu did not encounter strong opponents in the preliminary round, and his results were slightly worse. In the quarterfinals, Shepperd Han achieved only 23 seconds, defeating the American general Yellach. Huang Feilong finished third. Cheng Jinguan defeated Dong Yinchu and Lava Fu, with a time of 23.2 seconds. There will definitely be a fierce battle in the final, as their strengths are not far apart. Generally, Shepperd Han may win the championship, Yellach will be second, Cheng Jinguan third, and the remaining three will compete for fourth. Spring and Autumn

Random Thoughts on Loquats 226

— Zhan Lu

Loquats are yellow, the young and old hide them, the nanny is busy. I don't know who made this nine-character nursery rhyme, but it is a wonderful saying with great value for circulation. Du Mu's "The six states being defeated, the world united; the mountains of Shu being rugged, the Afang Palace arising," is not as natural and interesting as the three sentences of "Loquats are yellow." Someone said, "When depicting singing girls, why necessarily use singing girls, so the wonder of this nine-character nursery rhyme lies in using "Loquats are yellow" as a lead-in."

Shen Shitian's friend sent loquats as a gift, mistakenly writing it as pipa. Shitian replied in a letter: "Thank you for the pipa, opening the box was quite a shock; listening to it is silent, eating it is flavorful. Now I understand why Sima cried at Xunyang in ancient times, and Mingfei complained on the borderlands, all for the sake of a bite." The words in the old man Shitian's letter are extremely humorous. According to this, the names pipa and loquat could be used interchangeably in ancient times, but writing pipa as loquat is acceptable, while writing loquat as pipa is not. The old man Shitian's teasing words are not abusive.

The Compilation of Chicken Ribs records seedless loquats in Guangzhou, indicating that seedless loquats are not a rare species. Zhu Zhuotuo from Xiushui was friendly with a Taoist priest. There were two loquat trees in the Taoist temple. When the fruits were ripe, he picked them and sent them to Zhu, all of which were seedless. Zhu asked the Taoist priest about the planting method. The Taoist priest said, "The immortals planted them." Zhu didn't believe it. Knowing that the Taoist priest liked to eat steamed pork, Zhu invited the Taoist priest to drink and ordered a servant to buy a pig's trotter, deliberately letting the Taoist priest see it. In no time, the pig's trotter was cooked. When served to the guests, the meat was fragrant and particularly delicious. The Taoist priest asked Zhu, "How can it be cooked so quickly?" Zhu said, "I have a method to cook pig trotters in an instant." The Taoist priest asked to be taught this method. Zhu said, "Please exchange the method of planting seedless loquats with me." The Taoist priest said, "Easy, easy. When the flowers bloom, pluck out a pistil from the center, and the result will be seedless. I have already taught you. Please teach me the method of cooking pig trotters in an instant." Zhu said, "The pig trotters that the servant bought have not been cooked yet. What you just ate was cooked the previous night." After saying this, host and guest clapped their hands and burst into laughter.

On Dogs 227

— Jun Ti

Almost every household keeps a dog, or two or three. Except for foreign women, who keep them as pets, or for other needs, most are used to guard the house at night.

When it comes to the responsibility of a dog, guarding the house at night is also not small, but they never neglect their duty. First, they watch the door during the day or guard at night, and when they hear a knock, they bark loudly. Although they do not rest their heads on spears, they can be ready for orders. Second, within a household, they will never listen to one person's command to bite another. Third, when they hear the call of their kind, unless they are tied with a leash or locked in a cage, they will definitely run out to help. Even if they cannot go out, they will jump and bark wildly, remotely voicing their support. And it is heartfelt support.

From this, we know that although dogs are lower animals, they are loyal to their owners, loyal to their responsibilities, and full of mutual assistance.

We, who are called the soul of all things, should, in theory, be much higher than them. At the very least, we should be like them. Who knew we would be worse than them. There are many people whose responsibility is equal to that of a dog: watching the door and guarding the night. But when they hear a knock, they don't make a sound. When they see strangers, they seem to know them well, tucking their tails between their legs and turning away. However, within a household, they can listen to commands and bite people indiscriminately, with extreme ferocity, like a mad dog. Now, chased from outside the gate to the corner of the wall, although they are barking, they dare not bite back even once. Their kind—the soul of all things in the world—is not tied with a leash, nor is it locked in a cage, and although a few bark twice behind the door—it is not sincere support—they are never willing to come out to jump a few times or bite a few times.

We know that many of these people are not loyal to their owners, not loyal to their responsibilities, and have no spirit of mutual assistance for their kind. They cannot be equal to dogs, and perhaps they are not even as good as dogs. Therefore, now China does not necessarily need people, but cannot do without dogs; cannot do without sincere, loving, loyal, brave, and mutually assisting dogs!

Woman's Guardian

Chatting About Cartoons 228

(Text by Qian Yun)

(Art by Dong Liang)

Rights and obligations are undoubtedly relative, but enjoying rights does not necessarily mean being loyal to one's obligations. Only women's guardians, loyal ministers, and filial sons stand side by side, helping them take off their shoes, put on clothes, wash small handkerchiefs, and prepare milk at home; wherever they are, they are afraid of hurting even a single hair on their precious ones; even though they only have a pair of bare hands, is their power any different from those who hold guns? Sometimes it causes jealousy, especially among single men, right? Or harboring some kind of mentality, pretending not to see it, right? Women are always standing on proud ground.

Interesting Talk About Cigarettes 229

— Zui Chi Sheng

"A cigarette after a meal is better than being a god," those who enjoy smoking naturally have such an attitude. In fact, after drinking and tea, early in the morning and late at night, are the best times to smoke; it's truly "a cigarette in hand, feeling like an immortal."

I have never smoked. No matter how high-quality the cigarette, I can't understand it and dare not touch my lips. It can be said that I have no connection with cigarettes. But saying I have no connection is like I do; because you are always surrounded by cigarettes in public places, trapping you in an atmosphere of smoke. It makes you dizzy and unable to escape. Especially when playing mahjong with friends. They smoke constantly and throw the leftover cigarette butts on the ground. The smell of cigarette urine is even more unpleasant. Sometimes I say to them, "You invite me to play mahjong. No matter how clever your tactics, I'm not afraid. Only when you unite and launch a 'smoke screen' am I really a little scared." Everyone laughs when I say that!

Although I don't smoke, I often hold a cigar in my fingers. This also "Jesus has his reasons." Because when you are out, if people ask you to smoke, it seems inhuman to refuse. Secretly, they will inevitably say you are a fool who can't even smoke. So I thought of a way: take a cigar as a "block." Then, looking dignified, people will no longer offer you cigarettes. However, this cigar must be held in hand for at least a week or two weeks.

Some smoking friends do not discard the leftover cigarette butts. First, they gently tap the whole cigarette on the table a few times, and then moisten the cigarette butt with saliva and stick it back on. This is repeated over and over, leaving no residue. This kind of waste utilization can be considered the most economical way to smoke. But the poor man "catching crickets" who sees this will inevitably shake his head and sigh, saying that there is no way to make a living anymore (picking up cigarette butts on the road is called "catching crickets" in slang).

The most fun is smoking with a lover. The man takes a puff and passes it to the woman. The woman takes a puff and passes it back to the man, breathing each other's breath. But if others see it, they will always say you are "being sickening for fun."

People who are addicted to smoking always have some traces of being burned by cigarette ash on their clothes, indicating their smoking achievements. But even if you don't smoke, others will leave you some souvenirs. One day, I wore a brand new mandarin jacket to the bookstore to listen to a story, sitting upright, looking like "sacred and inviolable." Unexpectedly, when I got home, I found two cigarette burns on the back of the jacket. Besides saying a few words of pity, there was no other way. This was truly a "causeless disaster"!

Long Novel

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 230

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 8: Angry Words Provoke Youth to Resign and Flee, Enthusiastic Pity for Young Girl Brings Padded Clothing in Person

Houzhi sat at his desk, hands pressed on the table, eyes wide open, staring at people, making a show of exerting all his strength. Jizhi could only hang his hands down and stand straight at the corner, waiting for his older brother to finish scolding. However, Houzhi's last word, "scram," was not something he could endure. His face red, he said, "I haven't committed any major mistake, so why should I be told to scram?" Jizhi slammed the table and said, "I'm telling you to scram, what can you do about it?" Jizhi didn't say anything more, immediately walked out, returned to his own office, took a piece of draft paper, and hurriedly wrote a resignation letter on the table, saying: "Respectfully Submitted: Jizhi, holding a subordinate position, follows the law and regulations, and believes that there is no great fault. However, the director has repeatedly rebuked and shown no kindness. Reflecting on myself, I cannot understand the reason. Perhaps because Jizhi is suspected of bias toward people or matters, and treads upon the director's rule of avoiding relatives in appointments, I will draw the firewood from under the cauldron, and then boil beans to burn the stalks. A brave man cuts off his wrist, and it is not without necessity. Jizhi has read books and knows how to love himself. I am not willing to receive the grievances of three anxieties for the sake of one branch's existence. Therefore, I respectfully request to be relieved of my position as section member, to preserve Jizhi's personality, and to slightly relieve the director's burden. In closing, I am filled with extreme fear. Respectfully submitted to the Director. Section Member Gan Jizhi respectfully presents."

After Jizhi had copied it neatly, he gave it to the errand boy and asked him to send it to the director. He put on his coat and immediately walked out of the yamen, heading home. At this time, he felt that the sky was wide and the sea was vast, and he could go anywhere, completely free from any restrictions. His heart felt much better. When he got home, he ignored everyone, quickly checked his suitcases, and rolled up his luggage. He was packing in the room for an hour before the old nanny came in to bring boiled water, only then seeing this situation. She was very surprised and asked, "Second Master, what are you doing?" Jizhi smiled and said, "Nothing at all." The old nanny said, "Since you are doing nothing, why are you rolling up your luggage and packing your suitcases? It seems like you are going out. Where are you going?" Jizhi smiled and said, "Where am I going? Even I can't say for sure." The old nanny said, "If you can't say where you are going, why are you moving away?" Jizhi smiled and said, "Don't you know this? This is not my home!" (89)

Children's Paradise

Works by Two Little Friends 231

— Zhou Zheng

(A Message to Mr. Sun Yat-sen) Mr. Sun Yat-sen, it has been eight years since you left this world. In these eight years, do you know how our Republic of China is now? Do you know, Mr. Sun? I think you will definitely answer without hesitation: "The current Republic of China has already embarked on the right track, and has also realized the Three Principles of the People, the Five-Power Constitution, the Founding Strategy, and the Founding Outline. The warlords in the country have been overthrown, and both foreign and internal conflicts have been extinguished. The unequal treaties have also been abolished. The country is rich, and the people's livelihood is not impoverished." Alas, Mr. Sun Yat-sen! You know this is completely wrong. The current China is in a time of urgent foreign troubles. The three northeastern provinces and all of Rehe have been replaced by the Rising Sun flag. The warlords in the country have made a beautiful China look like a mess. Mr. Sun Yat-sen, are you not sad when you hear what I say? I think you must feel sad. The cute autumn begonia leaf has a corner eaten by insects. This is so unfortunate! (Zhang Jiaju)

(Hell on Earth) The compassionate Spring God has been working hard for many days like arrows, tidying everything up, leaving the world of mortals, and going to bed to rest quietly. The cruel Summer God, awakening in that hazy sleeping place, led his children, Mr. Sun and Miss Dewdrop, staggering to the world of mortals.

On the west side of that prosperous metropolis, there was a tragic sound, from that dilapidated thatched cottage, sobbing and moaning, chasing away the silent demons.

A young man wearing a dark green suit and a stiff shirt walked leisurely forward, passing by the door of the house. An old woman, half a century old, with wrinkles on her face like waves, knelt in front of the young man at the door, grabbed him, and cried: "Young master! Please do a good deed and save the poor. My son died today. Our whole family relies on him for food. Since he died, how can we survive? We also have no money for burial. What can we do? Please have some mercy and save the poor!" The young man said: "Get lost! You poor ghosts! How can a rich young man like me talk to you poor ghosts? Get lost! Get lost! Get lost!" He patted off the handprints on his pants and went to the dance hall without even turning his head. (Zhou Zheng)

(Oppression) In a prosperous and lively city, it was at the beginning of dawn. In a thatched cottage on the east side of the city, there was an old woman with snow-white eyebrows and hair, next to a young child, wailing and crying for something to eat, but the old woman's two oily eyes were shining on the pot, "Is there anything?" There wasn't! It had already been eaten, not even half a grain of rice left. Two hot tears kept flowing from her eye sockets.

A rent collector, with a big belly, a few rat whiskers beside his mouth, and a leather bag in his hand, strode into the thatched cottage.

Entering the door, he shouted loudly, "Twelve yuan for this month's rent, quickly pay up! There can be no arrears this month!"

Sobbing, she said, "Sir...sir, save...save my life, I don't even have food, how can I have silvery dollars? Please spare my life!"

The rent collector raised his lips like hills and said, "Bullshit! Don't be too long-winded, quickly pay the money! No can do! No can do!"

The rent collector took the old woman to the station. The wretched old woman suffered the flavor of iron bars, washing her dry face with hot tears all day long. (Zhou Zheng)
